  PROPERTIES
  {
    OnPreReport=VAR
                  tryOutRec@1100525000 : Record 11012750;
                BEGIN
                  CRFilter := "Estimate Line NEW".GETFILTERS;
                  CompInfo.GET;
                  CompInfo.CALCFIELDS(Picture);
                  PictureCounter := 0;
                  CLEAR(WarningArr);

                  SubEstimateFilter := "Estimate Line NEW".GETFILTER("Sub-Estimate No.");

                  TryOutCode := TryOutRelationRec.GetTryOut('',"Estimate Line NEW".GETFILTER("Estimate No."),'','','','','',2);
                  IF TryOutCode <> '' THEN
                    TryOutQuote.GET(TryOutCode);

                  TryOutCode1 := TryOutRelationRec.GetTryOut('',"Estimate Line NEW".GETFILTER("Estimate No."),'','','','','',1);
                  IF TryOutCode1 <> '' THEN
                    IF tryOutRec.GET(TryOutCode1) THEN
                      TryOutDesc := tryOutRec.Description;

                  IF CompressReceiptLines THEN
                    CompressReceiptLinesTxt := 'Receptregels zijn verdicht';

                  EstimateRec.GET("Estimate Line NEW".GETFILTER("Estimate No."));
                  EstimatePrincipal.SETRANGE("Estimate No.",EstimateRec."No.");
                  IF EstimatePrincipal.FINDFIRST THEN;

                  CLEAR(TempRecipeLine);
                  TempRecipeLine.RESET;
                  TempRecipeLine.DELETEALL;

                  IF PrintToExcel THEN BEGIN
                    IF ISCLEAR(xlApp) THEN
                      CREATE(xlApp,FALSE,TRUE);
                    xlBook := xlApp.Workbooks.Add;
                    xlSheet := xlApp.Sheets.Add;
                    xlApp.DisplayAlerts := FALSE;
                    xlSheet.Name := 'Open begroting';
                    xlSheet.Select;
                    xlSheet.Range('A1:K1').MergeCells := TRUE;
                    xlSheet.Range('A1').Value := 'OPEN BEGROTING per onderdeel';
                    xlSheet.Range('A1').Font.Bold := TRUE;
                    xlSheet.Range('A1').Font.Size := 18;
                    xlSheet.Range('A3').Value := "Estimate Line NEW".FIELDCAPTION("Estimate No.");
                    xlSheet.Range('A3').ColumnWidth := 12.57;
                    xlSheet.Range('B3:F3').MergeCells := TRUE;
                    xlSheet.Range('B3').Value := FORMAT(EstimateRec."No.");
                    xlSheet.Range('G3').Value := 'Filter:';
                    xlSheet.Range('H3:K3').MergeCells := TRUE;
                    xlSheet.Range('H3:K3').Value := "Estimate Line NEW".GETFILTERS;
                    xlSheet.Range('M4:N4').MergeCells := TRUE;
                    xlSheet.Range('M4').Value := COMPANYNAME;
                    xlSheet.Range('A5').Value := 'Calculatie:';
                    xlSheet.Range('B5:F5').MergeCells := TRUE;
                    xlSheet.Range('B5').Value := EstimateRec.Description;
                    xlSheet.Range('H5:K5').MergeCells := TRUE;
                    xlSheet.Range('H5').Value := EstimateRec."Description 2";
                    xlSheet.Range('L6').Value := EstimateRec.FIELDCAPTION("Rate Group");
                    xlSheet.Range('M6').Value := FORMAT(EstimateRec."Rate Group");
                    xlSheet.Range('A6').Value := 'Trajectnr.:';
                    xlSheet.Range('B6:F6').MergeCells := TRUE;
                    xlSheet.Range('B6').Value := FORMAT(TryOutCode);
                    xlSheet.Range('G6').Value := 'Trajectnr.:';
                    xlSheet.Range('H6:K6').MergeCells := TRUE;
                    xlSheet.Range('H6').Value := FORMAT(TryOutQuote.Code);
                    xlSheet.Range('A7').Value := EstimateRec.FIELDCAPTION(Estimator);
                    xlSheet.Range('B7:F7').MergeCells := TRUE;
                    xlSheet.Range('B7').Value := EstimateRec."Name Estimator";
                    xlSheet.Range('G7').Value := 'Indiendatum:';
                    xlSheet.Range('H7:K7').MergeCells := TRUE;
                    xlSheet.Range('H7').Value := DateTxt;
                    xlSheet.Range('A8').Value := 'Kostenplaats:';
                    xlSheet.Range('B8:F8').MergeCells := TRUE;
                    xlSheet.Range('B8').Value := EstimateRec."Global Dimension 1 Code";
                    xlSheet.Range('G8').Value := 'Opdrachtgever';
                    xlSheet.Range('H8:K8').MergeCells := TRUE;
                    xlSheet.Range('H8').Value := EstimateRec."Customer No.";
                    RowNo := 10;
                  END;
                END;

    OnPostReport=VAR
                   SummarySheet@1100525003 : Record 11012172;
                   SummarySheetLine@1100525002 : Record 11012171;
                   SummarySheetCode@1100525001 : Code[20];
                   i@1100525000 : Integer;
                 BEGIN
                   IF (DiffNormCounter <> 0) AND (ShowNormSet) THEN BEGIN
                     IF DiffNormCounter = 1 THEN
                       MESSAGE(Text002,DiffNormCounter);
                     IF DiffNormCounter > 1 THEN BEGIN
                       MESSAGE(Text002a,DiffNormCounter);
                     END;
                   END;

                   IF ShowSummarrySheet THEN BEGIN
                     SummarySheet.SETRANGE("Estimate No.",EstimateRec."No.");
                     IF SummarySheet.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
                       IF CONFIRM(Text004,TRUE) THEN BEGIN
                         IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(0,SummarySheet) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
                           SummarySheetCode := SummarySheet.Summary;
                           SummarySheetLine.SETRANGE("Estimate No.",EstimateRec."No.");
                           SummarySheetLine.SETRANGE(Summary,SummarySheetCode);
                           IF SummarySheetLine.FINDSET THEN
                             REPORT.RUNMODAL(72644, TRUE, FALSE, SummarySheetLine);
                          END;
                       END
                     END ELSE
                       MESSAGE(Text003,EstimateRec."No.");
                   END;


                   IF PrintToExcel THEN BEGIN
                     xlSheet.Cells.Select;
                     xlSheet.Cells.EntireColumn.AutoFit;
                     xlApp.Visible := TRUE;
                   END;
                 END;

  }
  DATASET
  {
    { 1100525000;;DataItem;                  ;
               DataItemTable=Table11072072;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Estimate No.,Sub-Estimate No.,Part Group,Part,Line No.);
               ReqFilterHeadingML=ENU=Estimate Line OLD;
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               PNumber := 0;
                               DiffNormCounter := 0;
                               TempRecipeLine.RESET;
                               TempRecipeLine.DELETEALL;
                               LastFieldNo := FIELDNO(Part);

                               CLEAR(NormTxt);
                               IF PrintNorm THEN
                                 NormTxt := 'Norm/ eenheid';

                               CLEAR(HoursTxt);
                               IF PrintHours THEN
                                 HoursTxt := 'Uren Totaal';

                               CLEAR(LaborTxt);
                               IF PrintLabor THEN BEGIN
                                 LaborTxt := 'Arbeid Totaal';
                                 LaborSign := Euro;
                               END;

                               CLEAR(MaterialTxt);
                               IF PrintMaterial THEN BEGIN
                                 MaterialTxt := 'Materiaal Totaal';
                                 MaterialSigntxt := Euro;
                               END;

                               CLEAR(SubcontractTxt);
                               IF PrintSubcontract THEN BEGIN
                                 SubcontractTxt := 'Onderaann. Totaal';
                                 SubContractSign := Euro;
                               END;

                               CLEAR(PlantTxt);
                               IF PrintPlant THEN BEGIN
                                 PlantTxt := 'Materieel Totaal';
                                 PlantSign := Euro;
                               END;

                               CLEAR(TotalTxt);
                               IF PrintTotal THEN BEGIN
                                 TotalTxt := 'Totaal';
                                 TotalSign := Euro;
                               END;

                               CLEAR(BrAmntTxt);
                               IF PrintBrAmnt THEN BEGIN
                                 BrAmntTxt := 'Bruto materiaal/ eenheid';
                                 BrAmntSign := Euro;
                               END;

                               CLEAR(PercDiscTxt);
                               IF PrintPercDisc THEN BEGIN
                                 PercDiscTxt := 'Korting';
                                 PercDiscSign := Perc;
                               END;

                               CLEAR(PriceTxt);
                               IF PrintPrice THEN BEGIN
                                 PriceTxt := 'Materiaal / eenheid';
                                 PriceSign := Euro;
                               END;


                               PrintColumns := PrintNorm OR PrintHours OR PrintLabor OR PrintMaterial OR PrintSubcontract OR
                                               PrintPlant OR PrintTotal;

                               IF PrintColumns THEN
                                 TotalLbl := 'Totaal voor Onderdeel'
                               ELSE
                                 TotalLbl := 'Einde Onderdeel';

                               IF EstimateRec."Rate Group" <> '' THEN
                                 TarievenSet := EstimateRec."Rate Group";
                               IF EstimateRec."Norm Group" <> '' THEN
                                 NormenSet := EstimateRec."Norm Group";
                               IF (EstimateRec."Priority Purch Disc Term Grp 0" = '') AND (EstimateRec."Priority Purch Disc Term Grp 1" = '') THEN
                                 KortingLabel := Text001
                               ELSE
                                 KortingLabel := Text001a;

                               IF (EstimateRec."Priority Purch Disc Term Grp 1" > EstimateRec."Priority Purch Disc Term Grp 0") AND
                                 (EstimateRec."Priority Purch Disc Term Grp 2" > EstimateRec."Priority Purch Disc Term Grp 1") THEN
                                 KortingReeks := EstimateRec."Purch Discount Term Group 2";
                               IF (EstimateRec."Priority Purch Disc Term Grp 1" < EstimateRec."Priority Purch Disc Term Grp 0") AND
                                 (EstimateRec."Priority Purch Disc Term Grp 1" > EstimateRec."Priority Purch Disc Term Grp 0") THEN
                                 KortingReeks := 'Bedrijf';
                               IF (EstimateRec."Priority Purch Disc Term Grp 0" = '') AND (EstimateRec."Priority Purch Disc Term Grp 1" = '') AND
                                 (EstimateRec."Priority Purch Disc Term Grp 2" = '') THEN
                                 KortingReeks := 'Bedrijf';

                               EstimateRec.CALCFIELDS("Name Estimator","Customer Name");

                               DimValRec.SETCURRENTKEY(Code,"Global Dimension No.");
                               DimValRec.SETRANGE(Code,EstimateRec."Global Dimension 1 Code");
                               DimValRec.SETRANGE("Global Dimension No.",1);
                               IF DimValRec.FINDFIRST THEN;

                               //DefineSummarySheet
                               SummarySheetRec.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", "Estimate Line NEW".GETFILTER("Estimate No."));
                               IF SummarySheetRec.COUNT > 1 THEN BEGIN
                                 MESSAGE('Kies het juiste staartblad');
                                 IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(0,SummarySheetRec) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
                                   SummarySheetRec.GET(SummarySheetRec."Estimate No.", SummarySheetRec.Summary);
                                   CalcSurcharches(SummarySheetRec);
                                 END;
                               END ELSE BEGIN
                                 IF SummarySheetRec.COUNT = 1 THEN BEGIN
                                   SummarySheetRec.FINDFIRST;
                                   CalcSurcharches(SummarySheetRec);
                                 END;
                                 IF NOT SummarySheetRec.FINDFIRST THEN
                                   ERROR('Geen staartblad gekoppeld aan calculatie %1', "Estimate Line NEW".GETFILTER("Estimate No."))
                               END;

                               EstRec.GET("Estimate Line NEW".GETFILTER("Estimate No."));
                               EstRec.CALCFIELDS("Labor Sales Amount");
                               AllLabor := EstRec."Labor Sales Amount";
                               TotCorr := (GetAmnttotal('2180') + GetAmnttotal('3085') + GetAmnttotal('3295')); // + GetAmnttotal();

                               // Estimate Line OLD, Header (2) - OnPreSection()
                               IF TempEstim <> "Estimate No." THEN BEGIN
                                 TempEstim := "Estimate No.";
                                 CurrReport.PAGENO := 1;
                               END;

                               EstimateRec.CALCFIELDS("Customer Name", "Contact Name");

                               IF NOT TryOutQteDateBl THEN
                                 DateTxt := STRSUBSTNO('%1',FORMAT(AlternativeDate))
                               ELSE BEGIN
                                 DateTxt := STRSUBSTNO('%1',FORMAT(TryOutQuote."Register Date"));
                               END;

                               // Estimate Line OLD, GroupHeader (4) - OnPreSection()
                               FooterPrinted := FALSE;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  lvEstimateLine@1100525006 : Record 11072072;
                                  lvRecipeLine@1100525005 : Record 11072075;
                                  lvEstimateLineRec@1100525004 : Record 11072072;
                                  EstimateLine@1100525003 : Record 11072072;
                                  LastOccInt@1100525002 : Integer;
                                  i@1100525001 : Integer;
                                  EstimatePart@1100525000 : Record 11072073;
                                  TempCorrDec@1100525007 : Decimal;
                                BEGIN
                                  Counter += 1;
                                  // Estimate Line OLD, Header (3) - OnPreSection()
                                  IF PrintToExcel THEN
                                    IF Counter = 1 THEN BEGIN
                                      FOR ColNo := 1 TO 100 DO BEGIN
                                        CellCde[ColNo] := matrix(ColNo,RowNo);
                                      END;
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Value := 'Deelcalculatie:';
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Font.Size := 12;
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Value := "Sub-Estimate No.";
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Font.Size := 12;
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Value := "Sub-Estimate Description";
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Font.Size := 12;
                                      RowNo += 1;
                                      CurrReport.SHOWOUTPUT(FALSE);
                                    END;

                                  IF NOT (CalcB) AND (PrintSummaryBl) THEN BEGIN
                                    GenerateTempLines("Estimate No.");
                                    CalcB := TRUE;
                                  END;

                                  CLEAR(SubOperation);
                                  IF ("Sub Operation Code" <> '') AND (ShowSubProc) THEN BEGIN
                                    SubOperation.GET("Sub Operation Code");
                                  END ELSE
                                    SubOperation.INIT;

                                  IF (TempPartNo <>'') AND (TempPartNo <> Part) THEN BEGIN
                                    CLEAR(TempRecipeLine);
                                    TempRecipeLine.RESET;
                                    TempRecipeLine.DELETEALL;
                                    CountBl := FALSE;
                                  END;

                                  IF ("Line No." <> 0) AND ("Estimate Line NEW"."Norm Group" <> EstimateRec."Norm Group") THEN BEGIN
                                    IF (Quantity <> 0) AND ("Sub Operation Code" <> '') OR (Quantity <> 0) AND ("Norm Group" <> '') THEN
                                      DiffNormCounter := DiffNormCounter + 1;
                                  END;

                                  IF ("Line No." <> 0) AND (ShowNormSet) AND ("Estimate Line NEW"."Norm Group" <> EstimateRec."Norm Group") THEN BEGIN
                                    InsertNormDiffLine("Estimate Line NEW");
                                  END;

                                  IF (CompressReceiptLines) AND NOT (CountBl) THEN BEGIN
                                    lvEstimateLineRec.RESET;
                                    lvEstimateLineRec.SETRANGE("Estimate No.","Estimate No.");
                                    lvEstimateLineRec.SETRANGE("Sub-Estimate No.","Sub-Estimate No.");
                                    lvEstimateLineRec.SETRANGE("Part Group","Part Group");
                                    lvEstimateLineRec.SETRANGE(Part,Part);
                                    IF lvEstimateLineRec.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
                                      RecCounter := lvEstimateLineRec.COUNT;
                                      TempRecCounter := RecCounter;
                                      CountBl := TRUE;
                                    END;
                                  END;

                                  IF (CompressReceiptLines) AND (CountBl) THEN
                                    RecCounter := RecCounter - 1;

                                  IF CompressReceiptLines THEN BEGIN
                                    lvRecipeLine.INIT;
                                    IF "Estimate Line NEW".Recipe ='' THEN BEGIN
                                      InsertOrModifyTempRecLine(lvRecipeLine,"Estimate Line NEW",Quantity,Quantity) //MMA.n
                                    END ELSE BEGIN
                                      IF Quantity <> 0 THEN BEGIN
                                        lvEstimateLineRec.INIT;
                                        lvRecipeLine.RESET;
                                        lvRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Estimate No.","Estimate No.");
                                        lvRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Sub-Estimate No.","Sub-Estimate No.");
                                        lvRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Estimate Line","Line No.");
                                        lvRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Part Group","Part Group");
                                        lvRecipeLine.SETRANGE(Part,Part);
                                        lvRecipeLine.SETRANGE(Recipe,Recipe);
                                        lvRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Recipe Group","Recipe Group");
                                        IF lvRecipeLine.FINDSET THEN
                                          REPEAT
                                            InsertOrModifyTempRecLine(lvRecipeLine,lvEstimateLineRec,Quantity * lvRecipeLine.Quantity,Quantity); //MMA.n
                                          UNTIL lvRecipeLine.NEXT = 0;
                                      END;
                                    END;
                                  END;

                                  ItemCode := "Item No.";
                                  IF "Basic Item" <> '' THEN
                                    ItemCode := Manufacturer + ' ' + "Basic Item";
                                  IF "Trade Item" <> '' THEN
                                    ItemCode := "Vendor (Trade Item)" + ' ' + "Trade Item";
                                  IF Recipe <> '' THEN
                                    ItemCode := Recipe;

                                  TryOutCode := TryOutRelationRec.GetTryOut('',"Estimate No.",'','','','','',2);

                                  CALCFIELDS("Quantity Model Exist");

                                  IF (TempPart <> Part) OR (TempSubEstimate <> "Sub-Estimate No.") THEN BEGIN
                                    TempPart := Part;
                                    HoursTotal[1] := 0;
                                    LaborTotal[1] := 0;
                                    MaterialTotal[1] := 0;
                                    SubcontractTotal[1] := 0;
                                    PlantTotal[1] := 0;
                                    AmountTotal[1] := 0;
                                    GrossAmountTotal[1] := 0; //MMA.n
                                  END;

                                  IF TempSubEstimate <> "Sub-Estimate No." THEN BEGIN
                                    TempSubEstimate := "Sub-Estimate No.";
                                    HoursTotal[2] := 0;
                                    LaborTotal[2] := 0;
                                    MaterialTotal[2] := 0;
                                    SubcontractTotal[2] := 0;
                                    PlantTotal[2] := 0;
                                    AmountTotal[2] := 0;
                                    GrossAmountTotal[2] := 0; //MMA.n
                                  END;

                                  Price[1] := 0;
                                  NormDec[1] := 0;
                                  HoursDec[1] := 0;
                                  LaborDec[1] := 0;
                                  MaterialDec[1] := 0;
                                  SubcontractDec[1] := 0;
                                  PlantDec[1] := 0;
                                  TotalDec[1] := 0;
                                  DiscountPercDec[1] := 0;
                                  SurchDec := 0;
                                  GrossAmountDec[1] := 0; //MMA.n

                                  PartQuant := "Part Quantity";

                                  IF PrintNorm THEN
                                    NormDec[1] := Norm;

                                  IF PrintHours THEN BEGIN
                                    HoursDec[1] := ROUND(Hours * PartQuant,0.01);
                                    HoursTotal[1] += ROUND(Hours * PartQuant,0.01);
                                    HoursTotal[2] += ROUND(Hours * PartQuant,0.01);
                                  END;

                                  LaborDec[3] := 0;
                                  MaterialDec[3] := 0;
                                  SubcontractDec[3] := 0;
                                  PlantDec[3] := 0;
                                  TotalDec[3] := 0;

                                  IF Recipe <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                    lvRecipeLine.RESET;
                                    lvRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Estimate No.","Estimate No.");
                                    lvRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Sub-Estimate No.","Sub-Estimate No.");
                                    lvRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Estimate Line","Line No.");
                                    lvRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Part Group","Part Group");
                                    lvRecipeLine.SETRANGE(Part,Part);
                                    lvRecipeLine.SETRANGE(Recipe,Recipe);
                                    lvRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Recipe Group","Recipe Group");
                                    IF lvRecipeLine.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
                                      REPEAT
                                        CalcRecTot(lvRecipeLine);
                                      UNTIL lvRecipeLine.NEXT = 0;
                                    END;
                                    LaborDec[1] := LaborDec[3];
                                    LaborTotal[1] += LaborDec[3];
                                    LaborTotal[2] += LaborDec[3];
                                    MaterialDec[1] := MaterialDec[3];
                                    MaterialTotal[1] +=  MaterialDec[3];
                                    MaterialTotal[2] +=  MaterialDec[3];
                                    SubcontractDec[1] := SubcontractDec[3];
                                    SubcontractTotal[1] += SubcontractDec[3];
                                    SubcontractTotal[2] += SubcontractDec[3];
                                    PlantDec[1] := PlantDec[3];
                                    PlantTotal[1] += PlantDec[3];
                                    PlantTotal[2] += PlantDec[3];
                                    TotalDec[1] := PlantDec[1] + SubcontractDec[1] + MaterialDec[1] + LaborDec[1];
                                    TotalDec[2] := PlantDec[1] + SubcontractDec[1] + MaterialDec[1] + LaborDec[1];
                                    AmountTotal[1] += PlantDec[1] + SubcontractDec[1] + MaterialDec[1] + LaborDec[1];
                                    AmountTotal[2] += PlantDec[1] + SubcontractDec[1] + MaterialDec[1] + LaborDec[1];
                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                    IF "Labor Cost Amount" <> 0 THEN
                                      "Labor Cost Amount" += ("Labor Cost Amount" / AllLabor) * TotCorr;
                                    BEGIN
                                      LaborDec[1] := ((("Labor Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Lab1) * Lab2);
                                      LaborTotal[1] += ((("Labor Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Lab1) * Lab2);
                                      LaborTotal[2] += ((("Labor Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Lab1) * Lab2);
                                    END;
                                    BEGIN
                                      IF ("Line Status" = 'B') THEN
                                        CurrReport.SKIP;
                                      CASE "Cost Object Price" OF
                                        '200','210','211','212','290': BEGIN
                                          IF ("Line Status" <> 'K') AND ("Line Status" <> 'RI')  AND ("Line Status" <> 'RD')
                                            AND ("Line Status" <> 'VB') THEN BEGIN
                                            MaterialDec[1] :=  (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1a) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                            MaterialTotal[1] += (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1a) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                            MaterialTotal[2] += (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1a) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                          END;
                                          IF ("Line Status" = 'K') THEN BEGIN
                                            MaterialDec[1] :=  (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1a) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                            MaterialTotal[1] += (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1a) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                            MaterialTotal[2] += (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1a) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                          END;
                                          IF ("Line Status" = 'RI') OR ("Line Status" = 'RD') OR ("Line Status" = 'VB') THEN BEGIN
                                            MaterialDec[1] :=  ("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                            MaterialTotal[1] += ("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                            MaterialTotal[2] += ("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                          END;
                                        END;
                                        '201': BEGIN
                                          IF ("Line Status" <> 'K') AND ("Line Status" <> 'RI') AND ("Line Status" <> 'RD')
                                            AND ("Line Status" <> 'VB') THEN BEGIN
                                            MaterialDec[1] :=  (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1b) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                            MaterialTotal[1] += (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1b) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                            MaterialTotal[2] += (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1b) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                          END;
                                          IF ("Line Status" = 'K') THEN BEGIN
                                            MaterialDec[1] :=  (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1a) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                            MaterialTotal[1] += (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1a) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                            MaterialTotal[2] += (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1a) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                          END;
                                          IF ("Line Status" = 'RI') OR ("Line Status" = 'RD') OR ("Line Status" = 'VB') THEN BEGIN
                                            MaterialDec[1] :=  ("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                            MaterialTotal[1] += ("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                            MaterialTotal[2] += ("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                          END;
                                        END;
                                        '202': BEGIN
                                          IF ("Line Status" <> 'K') AND ("Line Status" <> 'RI') AND ("Line Status" <> 'RD')
                                            AND ("Line Status" <> 'VB') THEN BEGIN
                                            MaterialDec[1] :=  (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1c) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                            MaterialTotal[1] += (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1c) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                            MaterialTotal[2] += (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1c) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                          END;
                                          IF ("Line Status" = 'K') THEN BEGIN
                                            MaterialDec[1] :=  (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1a) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                            MaterialTotal[1] += (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1a) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                            MaterialTotal[2] += (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1a) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                          END;
                                          IF ("Line Status" = 'RI') OR ("Line Status" = 'RD') OR ("Line Status" = 'VB') THEN BEGIN
                                            MaterialDec[1] :=  ("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                            MaterialTotal[1] += ("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                            MaterialTotal[2] += ("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                          END;
                                        END;
                                        '203': BEGIN
                                          IF ("Line Status" <> 'K') AND ("Line Status" <> 'RI') AND ("Line Status" <> 'RD')
                                            AND ("Line Status" <> 'VB') THEN BEGIN
                                            MaterialDec[1] :=  (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1e) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                            MaterialTotal[1] += (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1e) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                            MaterialTotal[2] += (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1e) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                          END;
                                          IF ("Line Status" = 'K') THEN BEGIN
                                            MaterialDec[1] :=  (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1a) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                            MaterialTotal[1] += (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1a) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                            MaterialTotal[2] += (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1a) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                          END;
                                          IF ("Line Status" = 'RI') OR ("Line Status" = 'RD') OR ("Line Status" = 'VB') THEN BEGIN
                                            MaterialDec[1] :=  ("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                            MaterialTotal[1] += ("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                            MaterialTotal[2] += ("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                          END;
                                        END;
                                        '204': BEGIN
                                          IF ("Line Status" <> 'K') AND ("Line Status" <> 'RI') AND ("Line Status" <> 'RD')
                                            AND ("Line Status" <> 'VB') THEN BEGIN
                                            MaterialDec[1] :=  (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1d) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                            MaterialTotal[1] += (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1d) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                            MaterialTotal[2] += (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1d) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                          END;
                                          IF ("Line Status" = 'K') THEN BEGIN
                                            MaterialDec[1] :=  (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1a) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                            MaterialTotal[1] += (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1a) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                            MaterialTotal[2] += (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1a) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                          END;
                                          IF ("Line Status" = 'RI') OR ("Line Status" = 'RD') OR ("Line Status" = 'VB') THEN BEGIN
                                            MaterialDec[1] :=  ("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                            MaterialTotal[1] += ("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                            MaterialTotal[2] += ("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                          END;
                                        END;
                                        '205': BEGIN
                                          IF ("Line Status" <> 'K') AND ("Line Status" <> 'RI') AND ("Line Status" <> 'RD')
                                            AND ("Line Status" <> 'VB') THEN BEGIN
                                            MaterialDec[1] :=  (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1f) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                            MaterialTotal[1] += (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1f) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                            MaterialTotal[2] += (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1f) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                          END;
                                          IF ("Line Status" = 'K') THEN BEGIN
                                            MaterialDec[1] :=  (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1a) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                            MaterialTotal[1] += (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1a) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                            MaterialTotal[2] += (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1a) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                          END;
                                          IF ("Line Status" = 'RI') OR ("Line Status" = 'RD') OR ("Line Status" = 'VB') THEN BEGIN
                                            MaterialDec[1] :=  ("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                            MaterialTotal[1] += ("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                            MaterialTotal[2] += ("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                          END;
                                        END;
                                        '206': BEGIN
                                          IF ("Line Status" <> 'K') AND ("Line Status" <> 'RI') AND ("Line Status" <> 'RD')
                                            AND ("Line Status" <> 'VB') THEN BEGIN
                                            MaterialDec[1] :=  (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1g) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                            MaterialTotal[1] += (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1g) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                            MaterialTotal[2] += (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1g) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                          END;
                                          IF ("Line Status" = 'K') THEN BEGIN
                                            MaterialDec[1] :=  (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1a) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                            MaterialTotal[1] += (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1a) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                            MaterialTotal[2] += (((("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant) * Mat1a) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                          END;
                                          IF ("Line Status" = 'RI') OR ("Line Status" = 'RD') OR ("Line Status" = 'VB') THEN BEGIN
                                            MaterialDec[1] :=  ("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                            MaterialTotal[1] += ("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                            MaterialTotal[2] += ("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                          END;
                                        END;

                                      END;
                                    END;

                                    {BEGIN
                                      CASE "Cost Object Subcontracting" OF
                                        '300': BEGIN
                                          CASE "Line Status" OF
                                            'K': BEGIN
                                              SubcontractDec[1] := (((("Subcontracting Amount" * PartQuant) * Sub1a) * Sub2a) * Sub3a);
                                              SubcontractTotal[1] += (((("Subcontracting Amount" * PartQuant) * Sub1a) * Sub2a) * Sub3a);
                                              SubcontractTotal[2] += (((("Subcontracting Amount" * PartQuant) * Sub1a) * Sub2a) * Sub3a);
                                            END;
                                            'I': BEGIN
                                              SubcontractDec[1] := (((("Subcontracting Amount" * PartQuant) * Sub1e) * Sub2c) * Sub3c);
                                              SubcontractTotal[1] += (((("Subcontracting Amount" * PartQuant) * Sub1e) * Sub2c) * Sub3c);
                                              SubcontractTotal[2] += (((("Subcontracting Amount" * PartQuant) * Sub1e) * Sub2c) * Sub3c);
                                            END;
                                              ELSE BEGIN
                                                SubcontractDec[1] := (((("Subcontracting Amount" * PartQuant) * Sub1a) * Sub2a) * Sub3a);
                                                SubcontractTotal[1] += (((("Subcontracting Amount" * PartQuant) * Sub1a) * Sub2a) * Sub3a);
                                                SubcontractTotal[2] += (((("Subcontracting Amount" * PartQuant) * Sub1a) * Sub2a) * Sub3a);
                                              END;
                                          END;
                                        END;
                                        '301': BEGIN
                                          SubcontractDec[1] := (((("Subcontracting Amount" * PartQuant) * Sub1b) * Sub2a) * Sub3a);
                                          SubcontractTotal[1] += (((("Subcontracting Amount" * PartQuant) * Sub1b) * Sub2a) * Sub3a);
                                          SubcontractTotal[2] += (((("Subcontracting Amount" * PartQuant) * Sub1b) * Sub2a) * Sub3a);
                                        END;
                                        '302': BEGIN
                                          SubcontractDec[1] := (((("Subcontracting Amount" * PartQuant) * Sub1c) * Sub2a) * Sub3a);
                                          SubcontractTotal[1] += (((("Subcontracting Amount" * PartQuant) * Sub1c) * Sub2a) * Sub3a);
                                          SubcontractTotal[2] += (((("Subcontracting Amount" * PartQuant) * Sub1c) * Sub2a) * Sub3a);
                                        END;
                                        '303': BEGIN
                                          SubcontractDec[1] := (((("Subcontracting Amount" * PartQuant) * Sub1f) * Sub2a) * Sub3a);
                                          SubcontractTotal[1] += (((("Subcontracting Amount" * PartQuant) * Sub1f) * Sub2a) * Sub3a);
                                          SubcontractTotal[2] += (((("Subcontracting Amount" * PartQuant) * Sub1f) * Sub2a) * Sub3a);
                                        END;

                                        '320': BEGIN
                                          SubcontractDec[1] := (((("Subcontracting Amount" * PartQuant) * Sub1d) * Sub2b) * Sub3b);
                                          SubcontractTotal[1] += (((("Subcontracting Amount" * PartQuant) * Sub1d) * Sub2b) * Sub3b);
                                          SubcontractTotal[2] += (((("Subcontracting Amount" * PartQuant) * Sub1d) * Sub2b) * Sub3b);
                                        END;
                                      END;
                                    END;
                                    BEGIN
                                      CASE "Cost Object Plant" OF
                                        '400': BEGIN
                                          PlantDec[1] := (((("Plant Amount" * PartQuant) * Plnt1a) * Plnt2a) * Plnt3a);
                                          PlantTotal[1] += (((("Plant Amount" * PartQuant) * Plnt1a) * Plnt2a) * Plnt3a);
                                          PlantTotal[2] += (((("Plant Amount" * PartQuant) * Plnt1a) * Plnt2a) * Plnt3a);
                                        END;
                                        '401': BEGIN
                                          PlantDec[1] := (((("Plant Amount" * PartQuant) * Plnt1b) * Plnt2a) * Plnt3a);
                                          PlantTotal[1] += (((("Plant Amount" * PartQuant) * Plnt1b) * Plnt2a) * Plnt3a);
                                          PlantTotal[2] += (((("Plant Amount" * PartQuant) * Plnt1b) * Plnt2a) * Plnt3a);
                                        END;
                                        '402': BEGIN
                                          PlantDec[1] := (((("Plant Amount" * PartQuant) * Plnt1c) * Plnt2a) * Plnt3a);
                                          PlantTotal[1] += (((("Plant Amount" * PartQuant) * Plnt1c) * Plnt2a) * Plnt3a);
                                          PlantTotal[2] += (((("Plant Amount" * PartQuant) * Plnt1c) * Plnt2a) * Plnt3a);
                                        END;

                                      END;
                                    END;}
                                    IF PrintTotal THEN BEGIN
                                      TotalDec[1] := PlantDec[1] + SubcontractDec[1] + MaterialDec[1] + LaborDec[1];
                                      TotalDec[2] := PlantDec[1] + SubcontractDec[1] + MaterialDec[1] + LaborDec[1];
                                      AmountTotal[1] += PlantDec[1] + SubcontractDec[1] + MaterialDec[1] + LaborDec[1];
                                      AmountTotal[2] += PlantDec[1] + SubcontractDec[1] + MaterialDec[1] + LaborDec[1];
                                    END;
                                  END;


                                  IF NOT PrintPlant THEN BEGIN
                                    PlantDec[1] := 0;      PlantTotal[1] := 0;         PlantTotal[2] := 0;
                                  END;
                                  IF NOT PrintSubcontract THEN BEGIN
                                    SubcontractDec[1] := 0;    SubcontractTotal[1] := 0;   SubcontractTotal[2] := 0;
                                  END;
                                  IF NOT PrintMaterial THEN BEGIN
                                    MaterialDec[1] := 0;       MaterialTotal[1] := 0;      MaterialTotal[2] := 0;
                                  END;
                                  IF NOT PrintLabor THEN BEGIN
                                    LaborDec[1] := 0;       LaborTotal[1] := 0;      LaborTotal[2] := 0;
                                  END;

                                  IF PrintPrice THEN BEGIN
                                    IF (Quantity <> 0) AND ("Material Cost Amount" <> 0) THEN
                                      Price[1] := MaterialDec[1] / (Quantity * PartQuant);   //"Material Amount" / Quantity;  //;
                                  END ELSE
                                    Price[1] := 0;

                                  //IF PrintPercDisc THEN
                                  //  DiscountPercDec[1] := "Discount %";

                                  IF PrintSurch THEN
                                    SurchDec := "Surcharge %";

                                  IF PrintBrAmnt THEN BEGIN
                                    GrossAmountDec[1] := "Gross Price";
                                    GrossAmountTotal[1] += "Gross Price";
                                    GrossAmountTotal[2] += "Gross Price";
                                  END;
                                  //MMA.en

                                  lvEstimateLine.SETRANGE("Estimate No.","Estimate No.");
                                  lvEstimateLine.SETRANGE("Sub-Estimate No.","Sub-Estimate No.");
                                  lvEstimateLine.SETFILTER("Line Status",'NC');
                                  lvEstimateLine.SETFILTER(Quantity,'<>%1',0);
                                  IF lvEstimateLine.FINDFIRST THEN
                                    NCBool := TRUE
                                  ELSE
                                    NCBool := FALSE;

                                  //Hoeveelheden onderdeel
                                  IF PartQuant <> 1 THEN
                                    Quantity := Quantity * PartQuant;

                                  CLEAR(DescriptionTxt);
                                  IF "Line Status" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                    LineStatus := "Line Status";
                                    IF ("Line Status" = 'NC') AND (Quantity <> 0) THEN       //GB.24-03-2010;
                                      DescriptionTxt := STRSUBSTNO('***** BOVENSTAANDE REGEL NIET COMPLEET *****',"Estimate Line NEW".Part);
                                    END ELSE
                                      LineStatus := '';

                                  IF  (DescriptionTxt = '') AND (STRLEN(Description) > 48) THEN BEGIN
                                    FOR i := 48 DOWNTO 1 DO
                                      IF (COPYSTR(Description,i,1) = ' ')  AND (LastOccInt = 0) THEN
                                        LastOccInt := i;
                                    DescriptionTxt := COPYSTR(Description, LastOccInt + 1, STRLEN(Description) - LastOccInt);
                                    IF LastOccInt <> 0 THEN
                                      Description := COPYSTR(Description,1, LastOccInt -1);
                                  END;

                                  TempPartNo := Part;

                                  IF (CompressReceiptLines) AND (RecCounter = 0) THEN BEGIN
                                    PrintLines := TRUE;
                                    CountBl := FALSE;
                                  END;

                                  IF (Quantity = 0) AND ("Unit of Measure" <> '') AND NOT (CompressReceiptLines) AND NOT (PrintZeroLines)
                                    THEN CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF STRPOS(Description,'SNIT') <> 0 THEN BEGIN
                                    DiscountPercDec[1] := 0;
                                    GrossAmountDec[1] := 0;
                                    Price[1] := 0;
                                  END;

                                  IF (PrintSummaryBl) AND ("Rate Code" <> '') THEN BEGIN
                                    InsertOrModifyRates("Rate Code", HoursDec[1], LaborDec[1]);
                                  END;

                                  // Estimate Line OLD, GroupFooter (12) - OnPreSection() Begin
                                  IF TotalPartBl AND (NOT RoundTotals) THEN
                                    IF PrintZeroLines OR (LaborDec[1] <> 0) OR (GrossAmountDec[1] <> 0) OR (PrevEstimateLineOld."Material Sales Amount" <> 0) OR (PrevEstimateLineOld.Quantity <> 0) OR
                                     ((LaborDec[1] = 0) AND (GrossAmountDec[1] = 0) AND (PrevEstimateLineOld."Material Sales Amount" = 0) AND (PrevEstimateLineOld.Quantity = 0) AND (PrevEstimateLineOld."Unit of Measure" = ''))  THEN
                                      IF (PrevPart <> "Estimate Line NEW".Part) AND (PrevPart <> '') THEN
                                        IF PrintToExcel THEN BEGIN
                                          FOR ColNo := 1 TO 100 DO BEGIN
                                            CellCde[ColNo] := matrix(ColNo,RowNo);
                                          END;
                                          xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Value := TotalLbl;
                                          xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Value := PrevEstimateLineOld.Part;
                                          xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Value := PrevEstimateLineOld."Part Description";
                                          xlSheet.Range(CellCde[5]).Value := FORMAT(HoursTotal[1]);
                                          xlSheet.Range(CellCde[6]).Value := FORMAT(LaborTotal[1]);
                                          xlSheet.Range(CellCde[10]).Value := FORMAT(MaterialTotal[1]);
                                          xlSheet.Range(CellCde[11]).Value := FORMAT(SubcontractTotal[1]);
                                          xlSheet.Range(CellCde[12]).Value := FORMAT(PlantTotal[1]);
                                          xlSheet.Range(CellCde[13]).Value := FORMAT(AmountTotal[1]);
                                          RowNo += 1;
                                        END;
                                  // Estimate Line OLD, GroupFooter (12) - OnPreSection() End

                                  // Estimate Line OLD, GroupFooter (17) - OnPreSection() Begin
                                  IF TotalSubEstimateBl AND (NOT RoundTotals) THEN
                                    IF PrintToExcel THEN
                                     IF (PrevSubEstimateNo <> "Estimate Line NEW"."Sub-Estimate No.") AND (PrevSubEstimateNo <> '') THEN BEGIN
                                       FOR ColNo := 1 TO 100 DO BEGIN
                                         CellCde[ColNo] := matrix(ColNo,RowNo);
                                       END;
                                       xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Value := TotalFor + FIELDCAPTION("Sub-Estimate No.");
                                       xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Value := PrevEstimateLineOld."Sub-Estimate No.";
                                       xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Value := PrevEstimateLineOld."Sub-Estimate Description";
                                       xlSheet.Range(CellCde[5]).Value := FORMAT(HoursTotal[2]);
                                       xlSheet.Range(CellCde[6]).Value := FORMAT(LaborTotal[2]);
                                       xlSheet.Range(CellCde[10]).Value := FORMAT(MaterialTotal[2]);
                                       xlSheet.Range(CellCde[11]).Value := FORMAT(SubcontractTotal[2]);
                                       xlSheet.Range(CellCde[12]).Value := FORMAT(PlantTotal[2]);
                                       xlSheet.Range(CellCde[13]).Value := FORMAT(AmountTotal[2]);
                                       RowNo += 1;
                                     END;
                                  // Estimate Line OLD, GroupFooter (17) - OnPreSection() End


                                  // Estimate Line OLD, GroupHeader (5) - OnPreSection()
                                  IF PrintToExcel THEN
                                    IF PrintZeroLines OR (LaborDec[1] <> 0) OR (GrossAmountDec[1] <> 0) OR ("Material Sales Amount" <> 0) OR (Quantity <> 0) OR
                                      ((LaborDec[1] = 0) AND (GrossAmountDec[1] = 0) AND ("Material Sales Amount" = 0) AND (Quantity = 0) AND ("Unit of Measure" = ''))  THEN
                                      IF ((PrevPart <> "Estimate Line NEW".Part) AND (PrevPart <> '')) OR (Counter = 1) THEN BEGIN
                                        FOR ColNo := 1 TO 100 DO BEGIN
                                          CellCde[ColNo] := matrix(ColNo,RowNo);
                                        END;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Value := 'Onderdeel:';
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Font.Size := 12;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Value := Part;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Font.Size := 12;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Value := "Part Description";
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Font.Size := 12;
                                        RowNo += 1;
                                      END;

                                  // Estimate Line OLD, GroupHeader (6) - OnPreSection()
                                  IF PrintToExcel THEN
                                    IF PrintZeroLines OR (LaborDec[1] <> 0) OR (GrossAmountDec[1] <> 0) OR ("Material Sales Amount" <> 0) OR (Quantity <> 0) OR
                                      ((LaborDec[1] = 0) AND (GrossAmountDec[1] = 0) AND ("Material Sales Amount" = 0) AND (Quantity = 0) AND ("Unit of Measure" = ''))  THEN
                                      IF ((PrevPart <> "Estimate Line NEW".Part) AND (PrevPart <> '')) OR (Counter = 1) THEN BEGIN
                                        FOR ColNo := 1 TO 100 DO BEGIN
                                          CellCde[ColNo] := matrix(ColNo,RowNo);
                                        END;
                                        xlSheet.Range(STRSUBSTNO('%1:%2', CellCde[1], CellCde[2])).MergeCells := TRUE;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).RowHeight := 33;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Value := 'Aantal';
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Font.Size := 12;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Value := 'Omschrijving';
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Font.Size := 12;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[4]).Value := NormTxt;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[4]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[4]).Font.Size := 12;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[5]).Value := HoursTxt;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[5]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[5]).Font.Size := 12;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[6]).Value := LaborTxt;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[6]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[6]).Font.Size := 12;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[7]).Value := BrAmntTxt;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[7]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[7]).Font.Size := 12;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[8]).Value := PercDiscTxt;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[8]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[8]).Font.Size := 12;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[9]).Value := PriceTxt;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[9]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[9]).Font.Size := 12;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[10]).Value := MaterialTxt;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[10]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[10]).Font.Size := 12;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[11]).Value := SubcontractTxt;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[11]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[11]).Font.Size := 12;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[12]).Value := PlantTxt;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[12]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[12]).Font.Size := 12;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[13]).Value := TotalTxt;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[13]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[13]).Font.Size := 12;
                                        xlSheet.Range(STRSUBSTNO('%1:%2', CellCde[1], CellCde[13])).WrapText := TRUE;
                                        RowNo += 1;
                                      END;


                                  // Estimate Line OLD, Body (8) - OnPreSection()

                                  IF PrintLineStatus THEN
                                    LineStatusTxt := "Line Status";

                                  IF Recipe <>'' THEN
                                    ReceiptID := 'R'
                                  ELSE
                                    ReceiptID := '';

                                  IF "Surcharge %" <> 0 THEN
                                    PercLabelSnit := Perc
                                  ELSE
                                    PercLabelSnit := '';

                                  IF PrintZeroLines AND
                                    ((LaborDec[1] = 0) AND (GrossAmountDec[1] = 0) AND ("Material Sales Amount" = 0) AND (Quantity = 0) AND ("Unit of Measure" = '')) AND
                                    ((LaborDec[1] <> 0) OR (GrossAmountDec[1] <> 0) OR ("Material Sales Amount" <> 0) OR (Quantity <> 0)) THEN
                                    IF PrintToExcel THEN BEGIN
                                      FOR ColNo := 1 TO 100 DO BEGIN
                                        CellCde[ColNo] := matrix(ColNo,RowNo);
                                      END;
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Value := FORMAT(Quantity);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Value := STRSUBSTNO('%1 %2', "Unit of Measure", LineStatusTxt);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Value := Description;
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[4]).Value := FORMAT(NormDec[1]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[5]).Value := FORMAT(HoursDec[1]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[6]).Value := FORMAT(LaborDec[1]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[7]).Value := FORMAT(GrossAmountDec[1]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[8]).Value := FORMAT(DiscountPercDec[1]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[9]).Value := FORMAT(Price[1]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[10]).Value := FORMAT(MaterialDec[1]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[11]).Value := FORMAT(SubcontractDec[1]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[12]).Value := FORMAT(PlantDec[1]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[13]).Value := FORMAT(TotalDec[1]);
                                      RowNo += 1;
                                    END;

                                  // Estimate Line OLD, Body (10) - OnPreSection()
                                  IF PrintLineStatus THEN
                                    LineStatusTxt := "Line Status";

                                  IF Recipe <>'' THEN
                                    ReceiptID := 'R'
                                  ELSE
                                    ReceiptID := '';

                                  IF "Surcharge %" <> 0 THEN
                                    PercLabelSnit := Perc
                                  ELSE
                                    PercLabelSnit := '';

                                  IF PrintZeroLines OR (LaborDec[1] <> 0) OR (GrossAmountDec[1] <> 0) OR ("Material Sales Amount" <> 0) OR (Quantity <> 0) OR
                                    ((LaborDec[1] = 0) AND (GrossAmountDec[1] = 0) AND ("Material Sales Amount" = 0) AND (Quantity = 0) AND ("Unit of Measure" = ''))  THEN
                                    IF PrintToExcel THEN BEGIN
                                      FOR ColNo := 1 TO 100 DO BEGIN
                                        CellCde[ColNo] := matrix(ColNo,RowNo);
                                      END;
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Value := FORMAT(Quantity);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Value := STRSUBSTNO('%1 %2', "Unit of Measure", LineStatusTxt);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Value := Description;
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[4]).Value := FORMAT(NormDec[1]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[5]).Value := FORMAT(HoursDec[1]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[6]).Value := FORMAT(LaborDec[1]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[7]).Value := FORMAT(GrossAmountDec[1]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[8]).Value := FORMAT(DiscountPercDec[1]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[9]).Value := FORMAT(Price[1]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[10]).Value := FORMAT(MaterialDec[1]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[11]).Value := FORMAT(SubcontractDec[1]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[12]).Value := FORMAT(PlantDec[1]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[13]).Value := FORMAT(TotalDec[1]);
                                      RowNo += 1;
                                    END;


                                  PictureCounter += 1;
                                  IF PictureCounter > 1 THEN
                                    CLEAR(CompInfo.Picture);

                                  // Estimate Line OLD, GroupFooter (12) - OnPreSection()
                                  CLEAR(CorrFactPartText);
                                  CheckCorrFactPart("Estimate No.","Sub-Estimate No.","Part Group",Part);
                                  //MMA.sn
                                  CLEAR(CorrFactText);
                                  CheckCorrFactSubEst("Estimate No.","Sub-Estimate No.",FALSE, Part);
                                  //MMA.en

                                  IF TotalPartBl AND (NOT RoundTotals) THEN  BEGIN
                                    ValueDec[2] := LaborTotal[1];
                                    ValueDec[3] := MaterialTotal[1];
                                    ValueDec[4] := SubcontractTotal[1];
                                    ValueDec[5] := PlantTotal[1];
                                    ValueDec[6] := AmountTotal[1];
                                    InsertTempEstPartPartRec(ValueDec, "Sub-Estimate No.", Part, "Part Description");
                                  END;

                                  // Estimate Line OLD, GroupFooter (15) - OnPreSection()
                                  CorrDec := 0;
                                  IF (AdjFactorHours <> 0) THEN
                                    CorrDec := HoursTotal[1] - (HoursTotal[1]/AdjFactorHours);
                                  //MMA.en

                                  IF (CorrFactPartText <> '') THEN BEGIN
                                    CorrCounter := CorrCounter + 1;
                                    CorrPartArr[CorrCounter] := CorrDec;
                                    PartArr[CorrCounter] := Part;
                                  END;

                                  // Estimate Line OLD, GroupFooter (16) - OnPreSection()
                                  TempCorrDec := HoursTotal[1] + -(CorrDec);
                                  CorrDec := 0;

                                  IF (AdjFactorHoursFact <> 0) THEN BEGIN
                                    CorrDec := TempCorrDec - (TempCorrDec / AdjFactorHoursFact);
                                  END;

                                  // Estimate Line OLD, GroupFooter (17) - OnPreSection()
                                  CLEAR(CorrFactText);
                                  CheckCorrFactSubEst("Estimate No.","Sub-Estimate No.",TRUE, Part);

                                  IF TotalSubEstimateBl AND (NOT RoundTotals) THEN BEGIN
                                    ValueDec[1] := HoursTotal[2];
                                    ValueDec[2] := LaborTotal[2];
                                    ValueDec[3] := MaterialTotal[2];
                                    ValueDec[4] := SubcontractTotal[2];
                                    ValueDec[5] := PlantTotal[2];
                                    ValueDec[6] := AmountTotal[2];
                                    InsertTempEstPartRec(ValueDec, "Sub-Estimate No.", "Sub-Estimate Description");
                                  END;

                                  // Estimate Line OLD, GroupFooter (19) - OnPreSection()
                                  IF CorrDec = 0 THEN
                                    IF (AdjFactorHoursFact <> 0) THEN
                                      CorrDec := HoursTotal[2] - (HoursTotal[2]/AdjFactorHoursFact);

                                  // Estimate Line OLD, Footer (20) - OnPreSection()
                                  IF NOT PrintPrintDate THEN
                                    DateLabelTxt := ''
                                  ELSE
                                    DateLabelTxt := 'Afdrukdatum/tijd: '+FORMAT(TODAY,0,'<day,2>-<month,2>-<year4>')+' / '+FORMAT(TIME,0,'<hours24,2>:<minutes,2>');

                                  IF PrintToExcel THEN BEGIN
                                    xlSheet.Cells.Select;
                                    xlSheet.Cells.EntireColumn.AutoFit;
                                  END;

                                  ShowEstimateLineOLD8 := (NOT CompressReceiptLines AND (PrintZeroLines OR (LaborDec[1] <> 0) OR (GrossAmountDec[1] <> 0) OR ("Material Sales Amount" <> 0) OR (Quantity <> 0)
                                                          OR ((LaborDec[1] = 0) AND (GrossAmountDec[1] = 0) AND ("Material Sales Amount" = 0) AND (Quantity = 0) AND ("Unit of Measure" = ''))));

                                  PrevSubEstimateNo := "Estimate Line NEW"."Sub-Estimate No.";
                                  PrevPart := "Estimate Line NEW".Part;
                                  PrevEstimateLineOld.COPY("Estimate Line NEW");
                                END;

               OnPostDataItem=BEGIN
                                // Estimate Line OLD, GroupFooter (12) - OnPreSection() Begin
                                IF TotalPartBl AND (NOT RoundTotals) THEN
                                    IF PrintToExcel THEN BEGIN
                                      FOR ColNo := 1 TO 100 DO BEGIN
                                        CellCde[ColNo] := matrix(ColNo,RowNo);
                                      END;
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Value := TotalLbl;
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Value := Part;
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Value := "Part Description";
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[5]).Value := FORMAT(HoursTotal[1]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[6]).Value := FORMAT(LaborTotal[1]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[10]).Value := FORMAT(MaterialTotal[1]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[11]).Value := FORMAT(SubcontractTotal[1]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[12]).Value := FORMAT(PlantTotal[1]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[13]).Value := FORMAT(AmountTotal[1]);
                                      RowNo += 1;
                                    END;
                                // Estimate Line OLD, GroupFooter (12) - OnPreSection() End

                                // Estimate Line OLD, GroupFooter (17) - OnPreSection() Begin
                                IF TotalSubEstimateBl AND (NOT RoundTotals) THEN
                                  IF PrintToExcel THEN BEGIN
                                    FOR ColNo := 1 TO 100 DO BEGIN
                                      CellCde[ColNo] := matrix(ColNo,RowNo);
                                    END;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Value := TotalFor + FIELDCAPTION("Sub-Estimate No.");
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Value := "Sub-Estimate No.";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Value := "Sub-Estimate Description";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[5]).Value := FORMAT(HoursTotal[2]);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[6]).Value := FORMAT(LaborTotal[2]);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[10]).Value := FORMAT(MaterialTotal[2]);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[11]).Value := FORMAT(SubcontractTotal[2]);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[12]).Value := FORMAT(PlantTotal[2]);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[13]).Value := FORMAT(AmountTotal[2]);
                                    RowNo += 1;
                                  END;
                                // Estimate Line OLD, GroupFooter (17) - OnPreSection() End
                              END;

               ReqFilterFields=Estimate No.,Sub-Estimate No.,Part Group,Part }
