    { 1100525002;1;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table11072075;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Estimate No.,Sub-Estimate No.,Part Group,Part,Estimate Line,Recipe Group,Recipe,Line No.);
               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  lvEstLineRec@1100525003 : Record 11012154;
                                  Quant@1100525002 : Decimal;
                                  lvEstLine@1100525001 : Record 11012154;
                                  SubEstPart@1100525000 : Record 11012153;
                                BEGIN
                                  IF ("Line No." <> 0) AND (ShowNormSet) AND ("Norm Group" <> EstimateRec."Norm Group") THEN BEGIN
                                    InsertNormDiffRecLine("Estimate Recipe Line");
                                  END;

                                  IF ("Line No." <> 0) AND ("Norm Group" <> EstimateRec."Norm Group") THEN BEGIN
                                    IF (Quantity <> 0) AND ("Sub Operation Code" <> '') OR
                                    (Quantity <> 0) AND ("Norm Group" <> '') THEN
                                      DiffNormCounter := DiffNormCounter + 1;
                                  END;

                                  SubEstPart.GET("Estimate No.","Sub-Estimate No.","Part Group",Part);

                                  IF CompressReceiptLines THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  CLEAR(SubOperation);
                                  IF ("Sub Operation Code" <> '') AND (ShowSubProcReceipt) AND NOT (CompressReceiptLines) THEN BEGIN
                                    SubOperation.GET("Sub Operation Code");
                                  END ELSE
                                    SubOperation.INIT;

                                  lvEstLineRec.GET("Estimate No.", "Sub-Estimate No.", "Part Group", Part, "Estimate Line");
                                  Quantity := Quantity * lvEstLineRec.Quantity;
                                  Hours := Hours * lvEstLineRec.Quantity;
                                  "Cost Amount" := "Cost Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity;

                                  ItemCode := "Item No.";
                                  IF "Basic Item" <> '' THEN
                                    ItemCode := Manufacturer + ' ' + "Basic Item";
                                  IF "Trade Item" <> '' THEN
                                    ItemCode := "Vendor (Trade Item)" + ' ' + "Trade Item";

                                  NormDec[2] := 0;
                                  Price[2] := 0;
                                  NormDec[2] := 0;
                                  HoursDec[2] := 0;
                                  LaborDec[2] := 0;
                                  MaterialDec[2] := 0;
                                  MatAmntDec := 0;
                                  SubcontractDec[2] := 0;
                                  PlantDec[2] := 0;
                                  TotalDec[2] := 0;
                                  GrossAmountDec[2] := 0;
                                  DiscountPercDec[2] := 0;
                                  PartQuant := lvEstLineRec."Part Quantity";

                                  //IF (PrintSummaryBl) AND ("Rate Code" <> '') THEN BEGIN
                                  //  InsertOrModifyRates("Rate Code", Hours, "Labor Amount");
                                  //END;

                                  IF PrintNorm THEN
                                    NormDec[2] := Norm;

                                  IF PrintHours THEN
                                      HoursDec[2] := ROUND(Hours * PartQuant,0.01);

                                  IF PrintLabor THEN BEGIN
                                    LaborDec[2] := ((("Labor Cost Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant) * Lab1) * Lab2);
                                  END;

                                  IF PrintMaterial THEN
                                      MaterialDec[2] := "Material Cost Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant;

                                  {IF PrintMaterial THEN BEGIN
                                    CASE "Cost Object Material" OF
                                      '200': MaterialDec[2] :=  (((("Material Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant) * Mat1a) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                      '201': MaterialDec[2] :=  (((("Material Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity *PartQuant) * Mat1b) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                      '202': MaterialDec[2] :=  (((("Material Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity *PartQuant) * Mat1c) * Mat1) * Mat2);
                                    END;
                                  END;

                                  IF PrintSubcontract THEN BEGIN
                                    CASE "Cost Object Subcontracting" OF
                                      '300': BEGIN
                                        CASE "Line Status" OF
                                          'K': SubcontractDec[2] := (((("Subcontracting Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant) * Sub1a) * Sub2a) * Sub3a);
                                          'I': SubcontractDec[2] := (((("Subcontracting Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant) * Sub1e) * Sub2c) * Sub3c);
                                            ELSE
                                              SubcontractDec[2] := (((("Subcontracting Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant) * Sub1a) * Sub2a) * Sub3a);
                                        END;
                                      END;
                                      '301': SubcontractDec[2] := (((("Subcontracting Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant) * Sub1b) * Sub2a) * Sub3a);
                                      '302': SubcontractDec[2] := (((("Subcontracting Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant) * Sub1c) * Sub2a) * Sub3a);
                                      '320': SubcontractDec[2] := (((("Subcontracting Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant) * Sub1d) * Sub2b) * Sub3b);
                                    END;
                                  END;


                                  IF PrintPlant THEN BEGIN
                                    CASE "Cost Object Plant" OF
                                      '400': PlantDec[2] := (((("Plant Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant) * Plnt1a) * Plnt2a) * Plnt3a);
                                      '401': PlantDec[2] := (((("Plant Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant) * Plnt1b) * Plnt2a) * Plnt3a);
                                    END;
                                  END;}

                                  IF PrintTotal THEN
                                    //TotalDec[2] := Amount * PartQuant;
                                    TotalDec[2] := PlantDec[2] + SubcontractDec[2] + MaterialDec[2] + LaborDec[2];

                                  //IF PrintPercDisc THEN
                                  //  DiscountPercDec[2] := "Discount %";

                                  //MMA.sn
                                  IF PrintBrAmnt THEN
                                    GrossAmountDec[2] := "Gross Price";
                                  //MMA.en

                                  IF PrintPrice THEN BEGIN
                                    IF (Quantity <> 0) AND ("Material Cost Amount" <> 0) THEN
                                      Price[2] := "Material Cost Amount"; // / Quantity;      25-10-2010
                                  END ELSE
                                    Price[2] := 0;

                                  MatAmntDec := "Material Sales Amount";

                                  IF PartQuant <> 1 THEN
                                    Quantity := Quantity  * PartQuant;

                                  CLEAR(DescriptionTxt);
                                  IF "Line Status" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                    LineStatus := "Line Status";
                                    IF ("Line Status" = 'NC') AND (Quantity <> 0) THEN       //GB.24-03-2010;
                                      DescriptionTxt := STRSUBSTNO('***** BOVENSTAANDE REGEL NIET COMPLEET *****');
                                    END ELSE
                                      LineStatus := '';

                                  IF (Quantity = 0) AND ("Unit of Measure" <> '') AND NOT (CompressReceiptLines) AND NOT (PrintZeroRecipeLines)
                                    THEN CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF STRPOS(Description,'SNIT') <> 0 THEN BEGIN
                                    DiscountPercDec[2] := 0;
                                    GrossAmountDec[2] := 0;
                                    Price[2] := 0;
                                    Quantity := 0.001;
                                  END;

                                  IF (PrintSummaryBl) AND ("Rate Code" <> '') THEN BEGIN
                                    InsertOrModifyRates("Rate Code", HoursDec[2], LaborDec[2]);
                                  END;

                                  // Recipe Line OLD, Body (2) - OnPreSection()

                                  IF PrintLineStatus THEN
                                    LineStatusTxt := "Line Status";

                                  IF "Surcharge %" <> 0 THEN
                                    PercLabelSnit := Perc
                                  ELSE
                                    PercLabelSnit := '';

                                  IF (PrintRecipeLines AND PrintZeroRecipeLines) OR (PrintRecipeLines AND (NOT PrintZeroLines) AND (Quantity <> 0) AND NOT (CompressReceiptLines)) THEN
                                    IF PrintToExcel THEN BEGIN
                                      FOR ColNo := 1 TO 100 DO BEGIN
                                        CellCde[ColNo] := matrix(ColNo,RowNo);
                                      END;
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Value := FORMAT(Quantity);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Value := STRSUBSTNO('%1 %2', "Unit of Measure", LineStatusTxt);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Value := Description;
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[4]).Value := FORMAT(NormDec[2]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[5]).Value := FORMAT(HoursDec[2]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[6]).Value := FORMAT(LaborDec[2]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[7]).Value := FORMAT(GrossAmountDec[2]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[8]).Value := FORMAT(DiscountPercDec[2]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[9]).Value := FORMAT(Price[2]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[10]).Value := FORMAT(MaterialDec[2]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[11]).Value := FORMAT(SubcontractDec[2]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[12]).Value := FORMAT(PlantDec[2]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[13]).Value := FORMAT(TotalDec[2]);
                                      RowNo += 1;
                                    END;
                                END;

               OnPostDataItem=BEGIN
                                TempRecipeLine.RESET;
                              END;

               DataItemLink=Estimate No.=FIELD(Estimate No.),
                            Sub-Estimate No.=FIELD(Sub-Estimate No.),
                            Part Group=FIELD(Part Group),
                            Part=FIELD(Part),
                            Recipe Group=FIELD(Recipe Group),
                            Recipe=FIELD(Recipe),
                            Estimate Line=FIELD(Line No.) }

               SourceExpr='RecipeLineOLDGroup' }

    { 1100525003;1;DataItem;ComprRecipeLines ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               TempRecCounter := TempRecCounter - 1;
                               TempRecipeLine.RESET;

                               SETRANGE(Number,1,TempRecipeLine.COUNT);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  lvEstLineRec@1100525000 : Record 11012154;
                                BEGIN

                                  IF Number = 1 THEN
                                    TempRecipeLine.FINDFIRST
                                  ELSE
                                    TempRecipeLine.NEXT;

                                  IF (TempRecipeLine."Sub Operation Code" <> '') AND (ShowSubProc) AND (CompressReceiptLines) THEN BEGIN
                                    SubOperation.GET(TempRecipeLine."Sub Operation Code");
                                  END ELSE
                                    SubOperation.INIT;

                                  //SubEstPart.GET(TempRecipeLine."Estimate No.",TempRecipeLine."Sub-Estimate No.",TempRecipeLine."Part Group",
                                  //              TempRecipeLine.Part);

                                  lvEstLineRec.GET(TempRecipeLine."Estimate No.", TempRecipeLine."Sub-Estimate No.",
                                    TempRecipeLine."Part Group", TempRecipeLine.Part, TempRecipeLine."Estimate Line");

                                  ItemCode := TempRecipeLine."Item No.";
                                  IF TempRecipeLine."Basic Item" <> '' THEN
                                    ItemCode := TempRecipeLine.Manufacturer + ' ' + TempRecipeLine."Basic Item";
                                  IF TempRecipeLine."Trade Item" <> '' THEN
                                    ItemCode := TempRecipeLine."Vendor (Trade Item)" + ' ' + TempRecipeLine."Trade Item";

                                  Price[2] := 0;
                                  NormDec[2] := 0;
                                  HoursDec[2] := 0;
                                  LaborDec[2] := 0;
                                  MaterialDec[2] := 0;
                                  SubcontractDec[2] := 0;
                                  PlantDec[2] := 0;
                                  TotalDec[2] := 0;
                                  GrossAmountDec[2] := 0;
                                  DiscountPercDec[2] := 0;
                                  PartQuant := lvEstLineRec."Part Quantity";


                                  IF PrintNorm THEN
                                    NormDec[2] := TempRecipeLine.Norm;

                                  IF PrintHours THEN
                                    HoursDec[2] := ROUND(TempRecipeLine.Hours * PartQuant,0.01);

                                  IF PrintLabor THEN
                                    LaborDec[2] := TempRecipeLine."Labor Cost Amount" * PartQuant;

                                  IF PrintMaterial THEN
                                    MaterialDec[2] := TempRecipeLine."Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant;

                                  IF PrintSubcontract THEN
                                    SubcontractDec[2] := TempRecipeLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount" * PartQuant;

                                  IF PrintPlant THEN
                                    PlantDec[2] := TempRecipeLine."Plant Cost Amount" * PartQuant;

                                  IF PrintTotal THEN
                                    TotalDec[2] := TempRecipeLine."Cost Amount"* PartQuant;

                                  //IF PrintPercDisc THEN
                                  //  DiscountPercDec[2] := TempRecipeLine."Discount %";

                                  IF PrintBrAmnt THEN
                                    GrossAmountDec[2] := TempRecipeLine."Gross Price"; //MMA.n

                                  IF PrintPrice THEN BEGIN
                                    IF (TempRecipeLine.Quantity <> 0) AND (TempRecipeLine."Material Cost Amount" <> 0) THEN
                                      Price[2] := TempRecipeLine."Material Cost Amount" / TempRecipeLine.Quantity;
                                  END ELSE
                                    Price[2] := 0;

                                  MatAmntDec := TempRecipeLine."Material Sales Amount";

                                  IF PartQuant <> 1 THEN
                                    TempRecipeLine.Quantity := TempRecipeLine.Quantity * PartQuant;

                                  CLEAR(DescriptionTxt);
                                  IF TempRecipeLine."Line Status" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                    LineStatus := TempRecipeLine."Line Status";
                                    IF (TempRecipeLine."Line Status" = 'NC') AND (TempRecipeLine.Quantity <> 0) THEN       //GB.24-03-2010;
                                      DescriptionTxt := STRSUBSTNO('***** BOVENSTAANDE REGEL NIET COMPLEET *****');
                                    END ELSE
                                      LineStatus := '';

                                  IF (TempRecipeLine.Quantity = 0) AND (TempRecipeLine."Unit of Measure" <> '') AND NOT (PrintZeroLines)
                                    THEN CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF STRPOS(TempRecipeLine.Description,'SNIT') <> 0 THEN BEGIN
                                    DiscountPercDec[2] := 0;
                                    GrossAmountDec[2] := 0;
                                    Price[2] := 0;
                                    TempRecipeLine.Quantity := 0.001;
                                  END;

                                  // ComprRecipeLines, Body (1) - OnPreSection()
                                  IF PrintLineStatus THEN
                                    LineStatusTxt := TempRecipeLine."Line Status";
                                END;
                                 }

    { 1100525004;;DataItem;                  ;
               DataItemTable=Table11012171;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Estimate No.,Summary,Row No.);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN

                               SETRANGE("Estimate No.", SummarySheetRec."Estimate No.");
                               SETRANGE(Summary, SummarySheetRec.Summary);
                               IF (VerdeelProjGebKstn) THEN
                                 SETFILTER("Row No.",
                                   '5510|5520|5550|6050|6100|6200|6550|6600|6700|6800|6850')
                               ELSE
                                 SETFILTER("Row No.",
                                   '4100|4200|4220|4250|4260|4300|4350|4400|4450|4550|4560|5510|5520|5550|6050|6100|6200|6550|6600|6700|6800|6850');

                               CurrReport.CREATETOTALS(Amount);

                               IF PrintToExcel THEN BEGIN
                                 xlSheet := xlApp.Sheets.Add;
                                 xlSheet.Name := 'Staartposten';
                                 xlSheet.Select;
                                 RowNo := 1;
                                 FOR ColNo := 1 TO 100 DO BEGIN
                                   CellCde[ColNo] := matrix(ColNo,RowNo);
                                 END;
                                 xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Value := 'Rubriek';
                                 xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                 xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Font.Size := 12;
                                 xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Value := 'Omschrijving';

                                 xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Font.Size := 12;
                                 xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Value := 'Bedrag';
                                 xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                 xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Font.Size := 12;
                                 RowNo += 1;
                               END;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  Temp@1100525001 : Decimal;
                                  Temp1@1100525000 : Decimal;
                                BEGIN

                                  CASE "Row No." OF
                                    '4100','4200','4220','4250','4260','4300','4350','4400','4450','4550','4560':
                                    BEGIN
                                      Temp := Amount + ((Amount / 100) * GetPerc('5050', "Estimate No.", Summary));
                                      Temp1 := Temp + ((Temp / 100) * GetPerc('5300', "Estimate No.", Summary));
                                      Amount := Temp1;
                                    END;
                                  END;

                                  IF Amount = 0 THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF PrintToExcel THEN BEGIN
                                      FOR ColNo := 1 TO 100 DO BEGIN
                                        CellCde[ColNo] := matrix(ColNo,RowNo);
                                      END;
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Value := "Row No.";
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Value := Description;
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Value := FORMAT(Amount);
                                      RowNo += 1;
                                    END;
                                END;

               OnPostDataItem=BEGIN

                                IF PrintToExcel THEN BEGIN
                                  FOR ColNo := 1 TO 100 DO BEGIN
                                    CellCde[ColNo] := matrix(ColNo,RowNo);
                                  END;
                                  xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Value := 'Totaal';
                                  xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Value := FORMAT(Amount);
                                  RowNo += 1;
                                  xlSheet.Cells.Select;
                                  xlSheet.Cells.EntireColumn.AutoFit;
                                END;
                              END;
                               }

    { 1100525006;1;DataItem;SamenvattingPart ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               TempEstPartRec.RESET;
                               TempEstPartRec.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", TempSubEstRec."Estimate No.");
                               TempEstPartRec.SETRANGE("Sub-Estimate No.", TempSubEstRec."Sub-Estimate No.");
                               TempEstPartRec.SETRANGE("Part Group", 'G');
                               SETRANGE(Number,1,TempEstPartRec.COUNT);
                               IF (TempEstPartRec.COUNT = 0) AND NOT (TotalPartBl) THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  IF Number = 1 THEN
                                    TempEstPartRec.FINDFIRST
                                  ELSE
                                    TempEstPartRec.NEXT;

                                  PartNumber += 1; //ROUND(TempEstPartRec.Quantity, 1); //+= 1; TempEstPartRec

                                  // SamenvattingPart, Body (1) - OnPreSection()
                                  IF TotalPartBl AND (NOT RoundTotals)  THEN
                                    IF PrintToExcel THEN BEGIN
                                      FOR ColNo := 1 TO 100 DO BEGIN
                                        CellCde[ColNo] := matrix(ColNo,RowNo);
                                      END;
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Value := TotalFor + 'onderdeel';
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Value := TempEstPartRec.Part;
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Value := TempEstPartRec.Description;
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[5]).Value := FORMAT(TotValuepDec[PartNumber][1]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[6]).Value := FORMAT(TotValuepDec[PartNumber][2]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[7]).Value := FORMAT(TotValuepDec[PartNumber][3]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[8]).Value := FORMAT(TotValuepDec[PartNumber][4]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[9]).Value := FORMAT(TotValuepDec[PartNumber][5]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[10]).Value := FORMAT(TotValuepDec[PartNumber][2] + TotValuepDec[PartNumber][3] +
                                        TotValuepDec[PartNumber][4] + TotValuepDec[PartNumber][5]);
                                      RowNo += 1;
                                      CurrReport.SHOWOUTPUT(FALSE);
                                    END;

                                  // SamenvattingPart, Body (2) - OnPreSection()
                                  IF TotalPartBl AND RoundTotals THEN
                                    IF PrintToExcel THEN BEGIN
                                      FOR ColNo := 1 TO 100 DO BEGIN
                                        CellCde[ColNo] := matrix(ColNo,RowNo);
                                      END;
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Value := TotalFor + 'onderdeel';
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Value := TempEstPartRec.Part;
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Value := TempEstPartRec.Description;
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[5]).Value := FORMAT(TotValuepDec[PartNumber][1]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[6]).Value := FORMAT(TotValuepDec[PartNumber][2]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[7]).Value := FORMAT(TotValuepDec[PartNumber][3]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[8]).Value := FORMAT(TotValuepDec[PartNumber][4]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[9]).Value := FORMAT(TotValuepDec[PartNumber][5]);
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[10]).Value := FORMAT(TotValuepDec[PartNumber][2] + TotValuepDec[PartNumber][3] +
                                        TotValuepDec[PartNumber][4] + TotValuepDec[PartNumber][5]);
                                      RowNo += 1;
                                    END;
                                END;
                                 }

    PROCEDURE InsertOrModifyTempRecLine@1000000017(RecipeLine@1000000000 : Record 11072075;EstLine@1000000001 : Record 11072072;MultiplyQty@1100525000 : Decimal;EstLineQuantity@1000000002 : Decimal);
    BEGIN
      IF RecipeLine."Estimate No." <> '' THEN BEGIN
        TempRecipeLine.RESET;
        TempRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Sub Operation Code",RecipeLine."Sub Operation Code");
        TempRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Trade Item",RecipeLine."Trade Item");
        TempRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Unit of Measure",RecipeLine."Unit of Measure");
        TempRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Line Status",RecipeLine."Line Status");
        TempRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Sub-Estimate No.", RecipeLine."Sub-Estimate No.");
        TempRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Part Group", RecipeLine."Part Group");
        TempRecipeLine.SETRANGE(Part, RecipeLine.Part);
        TempRecipeLine.SETRANGE(Description,RecipeLine.Description);
        IF TempRecipeLine.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
          TempRecipeLine.Quantity := TempRecipeLine.Quantity + (RecipeLine.Quantity * EstLineQuantity); // MultiplyQty); 16092001.GB
          TempRecipeLine."Material Cost Amount" := TempRecipeLine."Material Cost Amount" + (RecipeLine."Material Cost Amount" * EstLineQuantity);
          TempRecipeLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount" := TempRecipeLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount" + (RecipeLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount" * EstLineQuantity);
          TempRecipeLine."Labor Cost Amount" := TempRecipeLine."Labor Cost Amount" + (RecipeLine."Labor Cost Amount" * EstLineQuantity);
          TempRecipeLine."Plant Cost Amount" := TempRecipeLine."Plant Cost Amount" + (RecipeLine."Plant Cost Amount" * EstLineQuantity);
          TempRecipeLine.Hours := TempRecipeLine.Hours + (RecipeLine.Hours * EstLineQuantity);
          TempRecipeLine."Cost Amount" := TempRecipeLine."Cost Amount"+ RecipeLine."Cost Amount";
          TempRecipeLine.MODIFY;
        END ELSE
          CreateTempRecipeLine(RecipeLine,EstLineQuantity, EstLineQuantity); //MMA.n
      END ELSE BEGIN
        TempRecipeLine.RESET;
        TempRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Sub Operation Code",EstLine."Sub Operation Code");
        TempRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Trade Item",EstLine."Trade Item");
        TempRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Unit of Measure",EstLine."Unit of Measure");
        TempRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Line Status",EstLine."Line Status");
        TempRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Sub-Estimate No.", EstLine."Sub-Estimate No.");
        TempRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Part Group", EstLine."Part Group");
        TempRecipeLine.SETRANGE(Part, EstLine.Part);
        TempRecipeLine.SETRANGE(Description,EstLine.Description);
        IF TempRecipeLine.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
          TempRecipeLine.Quantity := TempRecipeLine.Quantity + EstLine.Quantity;
          TempRecipeLine."Material Cost Amount" := TempRecipeLine."Material Cost Amount" + EstLine."Material Cost Amount";
          TempRecipeLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount" := TempRecipeLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount" + EstLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount";
          TempRecipeLine."Labor Cost Amount" := TempRecipeLine."Labor Cost Amount" + EstLine."Labor Cost Amount";
          TempRecipeLine."Plant Cost Amount" := TempRecipeLine."Plant Cost Amount" + EstLine."Plant Cost Amount";
          TempRecipeLine.Hours := TempRecipeLine.Hours + EstLine.Hours;
          TempRecipeLine."Cost Amount":= TempRecipeLine."Cost Amount"+ EstLine."Cost Amount";
          TempRecipeLine.MODIFY;
        END ELSE
          CreateTempEstLine(EstLine);
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CreateTempRecipeLine@1000000022(RecipeLine@1000000000 : Record 11072075;MultiplyQty@1100525000 : Decimal;Qty@1000000001 : Decimal);
    BEGIN
      BEGIN //MMA.n
        TempRecipeLine.INIT;
        TempRecipeLine.COPY(RecipeLine);
        TempRecipeLine.Quantity := (TempRecipeLine.Quantity * Qty); // MultiplyQty); 16092001.GB
        TempRecipeLine."Cost Amount" := (RecipeLine."Cost Amount"* MultiplyQty);
        TempRecipeLine."Labor Cost Amount" := RecipeLine."Labor Cost Amount" * MultiplyQty;
        TempRecipeLine."Material Cost Amount" := RecipeLine."Material Cost Amount" * MultiplyQty;
        TempRecipeLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount" := RecipeLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount" * MultiplyQty;
        TempRecipeLine."Plant Cost Amount" := RecipeLine."Plant Cost Amount" * MultiplyQty;
        TempRecipeLine.Hours := RecipeLine.Hours * MultiplyQty;
        IF TempRecipeLine."Unit of Measure" = '' THEN
          TempRecipeLine."Unit of Measure" := "Estimate Line NEW"."Unit of Measure";//20-04-2010
        TempRecipeLine.INSERT;
      END; //MMA.n
    END;

    PROCEDURE CreateTempEstLine@1000000027(EstLine@1000000000 : Record 11072072);
    BEGIN
      BEGIN //MMA.n
        TempRecipeLine.INIT;
        TempRecipeLine."Estimate Line" := EstLine."Line No.";
        TempRecipeLine."Estimate No." := EstLine."Estimate No.";
        TempRecipeLine."Sub-Estimate No." := EstLine."Sub-Estimate No.";
        TempRecipeLine."Part Group" := EstLine."Part Group";
        TempRecipeLine.Part := EstLine.Part;
        TempRecipeLine."Sub Operation Code" := EstLine."Sub Operation Code";
        TempRecipeLine."Trade Item" := EstLine."Trade Item";
        TempRecipeLine."Unit of Measure" := EstLine."Unit of Measure";
        TempRecipeLine."Line Status" := EstLine."Line Status";
        TempRecipeLine.Quantity := EstLine.Quantity;
        TempRecipeLine.Norm  := EstLine.Norm;
        TempRecipeLine.Hours := EstLine.Hours;
        TempRecipeLine."Labor Cost Amount" := EstLine."Labor Cost Amount";
        TempRecipeLine."Material Cost Amount" := EstLine."Material Cost Amount";
        TempRecipeLine."Cost Object Price" := EstLine."Cost Object Price";// "Cost Object Material";
        TempRecipeLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount" := EstLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount";
        TempRecipeLine."Plant Cost Amount" := EstLine."Plant Cost Amount";
        TempRecipeLine."Gross Price" := EstLine."Gross Price";
        TempRecipeLine."Material Sales Amount" := EstLine."Material Sales Amount";  //GB.n
        TempRecipeLine."Subcontracting Sales Amount" := EstLine."Subcontracting Sales Amount";//GB.n
        TempRecipeLine."Cost Amount" := EstLine."Cost Amount";
        TempRecipeLine.Description := EstLine.Description;
        //TempRecipeLine."Discount %" := EstLine."Discount %"; //MMA.n
        TempRecipeLine.INSERT;
      END; //MMA.n
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckCorrFactSubEst@1000000002(Est@1000000001 : Code[20];SubEst@1000000002 : Code[20];EndLine@1000000003 : Boolean;Prt@1000000004 : Code[20]);
    VAR
      SubEstimaterRec@1000000000 : Record 11012152;
    BEGIN
      SubEstimaterRec.GET(Est,SubEst);
      IF (SubEstimaterRec."Adjustment Factor Hours" <> 1) AND (EndLine) THEN BEGIN
        CorrFactText := STRSUBSTNO(CorrTotalText,SubEstimaterRec."Adjustment Factor Hours",SubEst);
        AdjFactorHoursFact := SubEstimaterRec."Adjustment Factor Hours"; //MMA.n
      END ELSE
        IF (SubEstimaterRec."Adjustment Factor Hours" <> 1) AND NOT (EndLine) THEN BEGIN
          //CorrFactText := STRSUBSTNO(CorrText,SubEstimaterRec."Adjustment Factor Hours",SubEst);
          CorrFactText := STRSUBSTNO(CorrText1,SubEstimaterRec."Adjustment Factor Hours", Prt);
          AdjFactorHoursFact := SubEstimaterRec."Adjustment Factor Hours"; //MMA.n
        END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckCorrFactPart@1000000021(Est@1000000001 : Code[20];SubEst@1000000002 : Code[20];PartGroup@1000000004 : Code[20];Part@1000000003 : Code[20]);
    VAR
      SubEstimaterPartRec@1000000000 : Record 11012153;
    BEGIN
      SubEstimaterPartRec.GET(Est,SubEst,PartGroup,Part);
      IF SubEstimaterPartRec."Adjustment Factor Hours" <> 1 THEN BEGIN
        CorrFactPartText := STRSUBSTNO('Corectiefactor uren %1 % op onderdeel %2',SubEstimaterPartRec."Adjustment Factor Hours",Part);
        AdjFactorHours := SubEstimaterPartRec."Adjustment Factor Hours";
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE InsertNormDiffLine@1000000000(Estline@1000000000 : Record 11072072);
    BEGIN
      IF NOT ShowNormSet THEN
        EXIT;
      IF (Estline.Quantity <> 0) AND (Estline."Sub Operation Code" <> '') OR
       (Estline.Quantity <> 0) AND (Estline."Norm Group" <> '') THEN BEGIN
        TempNormDiffLine := Estline;
        TempNormDiffLine.INSERT;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE InsertNormDiffRecLine@1000000012(RecLine@1000000000 : Record 11072075);
    BEGIN
      IF NOT ShowNormSet THEN
        EXIT;

      IF (RecLine.Quantity <> 0) AND (RecLine."Sub Operation Code" <> '') OR
        (RecLine.Quantity <> 0) AND (RecLine."Norm Group" <> '')  THEN BEGIN
        TempNormDiffRecLine := RecLine;
        TempNormDiffRecLine.INSERT;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE GenerateTempLines@1000000003(EstimateNo@1000000000 : Code[20]);
    VAR
      SubEstimate@1000000001 : Record 11072074;
      SubEstimatePart@1000000002 : Record 11072073;
    BEGIN
      CLEAR(TempSubEstimateRec);
      TempSubEstimateRec.RESET;
      TempSubEstimateRec.DELETEALL;
      CLEAR(TempSubEstimatePartRec);
      TempSubEstimatePartRec.RESET;
      TempSubEstimatePartRec.DELETEALL;

      SubEstimate.SETRANGE("Estimate No.",EstimateNo);
      IF SubEstimate.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          SubEstimatePart.SETRANGE("Estimate No.",EstimateNo);
          SubEstimatePart.SETRANGE("Sub-Estimate No.",SubEstimate."Sub-Estimate No.");
          IF SubEstimatePart.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
            REPEAT
              TempSubEstimatePartRec := SubEstimatePart;
              TempSubEstimatePartRec.INSERT;
            UNTIL SubEstimatePart.NEXT = 0;
          END;
          TempSubEstimateRec := SubEstimate;
          TempSubEstimateRec.INSERT;
        UNTIL SubEstimate.NEXT = 0;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CALCsumm@1000000007();
    VAR
      EstimateLine@1000000000 : Record 11012154;
    BEGIN
      //Specifiek materiaal
      EstimateLine.SETRANGE("Estimate No.","Estimate Line NEW"."Estimate No.");
      IF SubEstimateFilter <> '' THEN
        EstimateLine.SETFILTER("Sub-Estimate No.",SubEstimateFilter);

      EstimateLine.SETFILTER("Line Status", 'S');
      IF EstimateLine.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          SpecMatDec[1] += EstimateLine."Material Amount";
        UNTIL EstimateLine.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      //Generiek materiaal
      EstimateLine.SETFILTER("Line Status", '<>S&<>P&<>V&<>RI&<>RD');
      IF EstimateLine.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          SpecMatDec[2] += EstimateLine."Material Amount";
        UNTIL EstimateLine.NEXT = 0;
      END;


      //Onderaanneming
      EstimateLine.SETFILTER("Line Status",'<>I');
      IF EstimateLine.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          SpecMatDec[3] += EstimateLine."Subcontracting Amount";
        UNTIL EstimateLine.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      //Imtech Divisie
      EstimateLine.SETFILTER("Line Status",'I');
      IF EstimateLine.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          SpecMatDec[4] += EstimateLine."Subcontracting Amount";
        UNTIL EstimateLine.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      //Stelposten
      EstimateLine.SETFILTER("Line Status",'P');
      IF EstimateLine.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          SpecMatDec[5] += EstimateLine."Material Amount";
        UNTIL EstimateLine.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      //Verrekenprijzen
      EstimateLine.SETFILTER("Line Status",'V');
      IF EstimateLine.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          SpecMatDec[6] += EstimateLine."Material Amount";
        UNTIL EstimateLine.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      //Reis en verblijfkosten
      EstimateLine.SETFILTER("Line Status",'RI|RD');
      IF EstimateLine.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          SpecMatDec[7] += EstimateLine."Material Amount";
        UNTIL EstimateLine.NEXT = 0;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE InsertOrModifyRates@1000000005(RateCode@1000000000 : Code[20];Hours@1000000001 : Decimal;Amount@1000000002 : Decimal);
    BEGIN
      //Project No.,Adjustment,Extension Contract,Option,Line No.
      TempEstimateRate.RESET;
      IF TempEstimateRate.GET("Estimate Line NEW"."Estimate No.", RateCode,'','',0) THEN BEGIN
        TempEstimateRate.Hours += Hours;
        TempEstimateRate.Amount += Amount;
        TempEstimateRate.MODIFY;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        TempEstimateRate."Project No." := "Estimate Line NEW"."Estimate No.";
        TempEstimateRate.Adjustment := RateCode;
        TempEstimateRate.Description := RateDesc(RateCode);
        TempEstimateRate.Rate := RateRate(RateCode);
        TempEstimateRate.Hours := Hours;
        TempEstimateRate.Amount := Amount;
        TempEstimateRate.INSERT;
        TempEstimateRate.RESET;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE RateDesc@1000000001(RateCode@1000000000 : Code[20]) : Text[50];
    VAR
      EstimateRateRec@1000000001 : Record 11012160;
    BEGIN
      IF EstimateRateRec.GET("Estimate Line NEW"."Estimate No.", RateCode) THEN
        EXIT(EstimateRateRec.Description);
    END;

    PROCEDURE RateRate@1000000011(RateCode@1000000001 : Code[20]) : Decimal;
    VAR
      EstimateRateRec@1000000000 : Record 11012160;
    BEGIN
      IF EstimateRateRec.GET("Estimate Line NEW"."Estimate No.", RateCode) THEN BEGIN
        CASE EstimateRateRec."Rate Type" OF
          EstimateRateRec."Rate Type"::Hours: EXIT(EstimateRateRec."Cost Rate");
          EstimateRateRec."Rate Type"::Minuts: EXIT(EstimateRateRec."Cost Rate" * (60 / EstimateRateRec."Team Size"));
        END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalcSurcharches@1000000020(SumSheetRec@1000000000 : Record 11012172);
    BEGIN
      //Arbeid
      Lab1 := 1 + (GetPerc('5045', SumSheetRec."Estimate No.", SumSheetRec.Summary) / 100);
      Lab2 := 1 + (GetPerc('5200', SumSheetRec."Estimate No.", SumSheetRec.Summary) / 100);
      IF Lab1 = 0 THEN  Lab1 := 1;
      IF Lab2 = 0 THEN  Lab2 := 1;

      //Materiaal     //'200','210','211','212','290'
      Mat1 :=  1 + (GetPerc('5020', SumSheetRec."Estimate No.", SumSheetRec.Summary) / 100);
      Mat2 :=  1 + (GetPerc('5100', SumSheetRec."Estimate No.", SumSheetRec.Summary) / 100);
      Mat1a := 1 + (GetPerc('1250', SumSheetRec."Estimate No.", SumSheetRec.Summary) / 100);  //200
      Mat1b := 1 + (GetPerc('1255', SumSheetRec."Estimate No.", SumSheetRec.Summary) / 100);  //201
      Mat1c := 1 + (GetPerc('1260', SumSheetRec."Estimate No.", SumSheetRec.Summary) / 100);  //202
      Mat1d := 1 + (GetPerc('1270', SumSheetRec."Estimate No.", SumSheetRec.Summary) / 100);  //204
      //n*
      Mat1e := 1 + (GetPerc('1265', SumSheetRec."Estimate No.", SumSheetRec.Summary) / 100);  //203
      Mat1f := 1 + (GetPerc('1275', SumSheetRec."Estimate No.", SumSheetRec.Summary) / 100);  //205
      Mat1g := 1 + (GetPerc('1280', SumSheetRec."Estimate No.", SumSheetRec.Summary) / 100);  //206

      IF Mat1 = 0 THEN Mat1 := 1;
      IF Mat2 = 0 THEN Mat2 := 1;
      IF Mat1a = 0 THEN Mat1a := 1;
      IF Mat1b = 0 THEN Mat1b := 1;
      IF Mat1c = 0 THEN Mat1c := 1;
      IF Mat1d = 0 THEN Mat1d := 1;
      IF Mat1e = 0 THEN Mat1e := 1;
      IF Mat1f = 0 THEN Mat1f := 1;
      IF Mat1g = 0 THEN Mat1g := 1;

      //Subcontracting
      Sub1a := 1 + (GetPerc('1350', SumSheetRec."Estimate No.", SumSheetRec.Summary) / 100);   //300
      Sub1b := 1 + (GetPerc('1360', SumSheetRec."Estimate No.", SumSheetRec.Summary) / 100);   //301
      Sub1c := 1 + (GetPerc('1370', SumSheetRec."Estimate No.", SumSheetRec.Summary) / 100);   //302
      Sub1d := 1 + (GetPerc('1380', SumSheetRec."Estimate No.", SumSheetRec.Summary) / 100);   //320
      Sub1e := 1 + (GetPerc('1385', SumSheetRec."Estimate No.", SumSheetRec.Summary) / 100);   //300i
      Sub1f := 1 + (GetPerc('1375', SumSheetRec."Estimate No.", SumSheetRec.Summary) / 100);   //303

      Sub2a := 1 + (GetPerc('5025', SumSheetRec."Estimate No.", SumSheetRec.Summary) / 100);
      Sub2b := 1 + (GetPerc('5030', SumSheetRec."Estimate No.", SumSheetRec.Summary) / 100);
      Sub2c := 1 + (GetPerc('5035', SumSheetRec."Estimate No.", SumSheetRec.Summary) / 100);
      Sub3a := 1 + (GetPerc('5150', SumSheetRec."Estimate No.", SumSheetRec.Summary) / 100);
      Sub3b := 1 + (GetPerc('5160', SumSheetRec."Estimate No.", SumSheetRec.Summary) / 100);
      Sub3c := 1 + (GetPerc('5170', SumSheetRec."Estimate No.", SumSheetRec.Summary) / 100);



      IF Sub1a = 0 THEN Sub1a := 1;
      IF Sub1b = 0 THEN Sub1b := 1;
      IF Sub1c = 0 THEN Sub1c := 1;
      IF Sub1d = 0 THEN Sub1d := 1;
      IF Sub1e = 0 THEN Sub1e := 1;
      IF Sub1f = 0 THEN Sub1f := 1;
      IF Sub2a = 0 THEN Sub2a := 1;
      IF Sub2b = 0 THEN Sub2b := 1;
      IF Sub2c = 0 THEN Sub2c := 1;
      IF Sub3a = 0 THEN Sub3a := 1;
      IF Sub3b = 0 THEN Sub3b := 1;
      IF Sub3c = 0 THEN Sub3c := 1;

      //Materieel
      Plnt1a := 1 + (GetPerc('1441', SumSheetRec."Estimate No.", SumSheetRec.Summary) / 100);  //400
      Plnt1b := 1 + (GetPerc('1442', SumSheetRec."Estimate No.", SumSheetRec.Summary) / 100);  //401
      Plnt1c := 1 + (GetPerc('1443', SumSheetRec."Estimate No.", SumSheetRec.Summary) / 100);  //402
      Plnt2a := 1 + (GetPerc('5040', SumSheetRec."Estimate No.", SumSheetRec.Summary) / 100);
      Plnt3a := 1 + (GetPerc('5180', SumSheetRec."Estimate No.", SumSheetRec.Summary) / 100);

      IF Plnt1a = 0 THEN Plnt1a := 1;
      IF Plnt1b = 0 THEN Plnt1b := 1;
      IF Plnt1c = 0 THEN Plnt1c := 1;
      IF Plnt2a = 0 THEN Plnt2a := 1;
      IF Plnt3a = 0 THEN Plnt3a := 1;
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetPerc@1000000024(RowNo@1000000000 : Code[10];EstNo@1000000001 : Code[20];Summ@1000000002 : Code[20]) : Decimal;
    VAR
      SummSheetLine@1000000003 : Record 11012171;

    PROCEDURE CalcRecTot@1000000068(RecLine@1000000000 : Record 11072075);
    VAR
      lvEstLineRec@1000000001 : Record 11012154;
    BEGIN
      WITH RecLine DO BEGIN
        lvEstLineRec.GET("Estimate No.", "Sub-Estimate No.", "Part Group", Part, "Estimate Line");
        IF PrintLabor THEN BEGIN
          IF "Labor Cost Amount" <> 0 THEN
            "Labor Cost Amount" += ("Labor Cost Amount" / AllLabor) * TotCorr;
          LaborDec[3] += ((("Labor Cost Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant) * Lab1) * Lab2);
        END;
        IF PrintMaterial THEN BEGIN
          CASE "Cost Object Price" OF
            '200': BEGIN
              IF ("Line Status" <> 'K') AND ("Line Status" <> 'RI')  AND ("Line Status" <> 'RD')
              AND ("Line Status" <> 'VB') THEN
                MaterialDec[3] +=  (((("Material Cost Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant) * Mat1a) * Mat1) * Mat2);
              IF ("Line Status" = 'RI') OR ("Line Status" = 'RD') OR ("Line Status" = 'VB') THEN
                MaterialDec[3] +=  ("Material Cost Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant)
            END;
            '201': BEGIN
            IF ("Line Status" <> 'K') AND ("Line Status" <> 'RI')  AND ("Line Status" <> 'RD')
                AND ("Line Status" <> 'VB') THEN
            MaterialDec[3] +=  (((("Material Cost Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant) * Mat1b) * Mat1) * Mat2);
            IF ("Line Status" = 'RI') OR ("Line Status" = 'RD') OR ("Line Status" = 'VB') THEN
              MaterialDec[3] +=  ("Material Cost Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant)
            END;
            '202': BEGIN
            IF ("Line Status" <> 'K') AND ("Line Status" <> 'RI')  AND ("Line Status" <> 'RD')
            AND ("Line Status" <> 'VB') THEN
              MaterialDec[3] +=  (((("Material Cost Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant) * Mat1c) * Mat1) * Mat2);
            IF ("Line Status" = 'RI') OR ("Line Status" = 'RD') OR ("Line Status" = 'VB') THEN
              MaterialDec[3] +=  ("Material Cost Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant)
            END;
            '203': BEGIN
            IF ("Line Status" <> 'K') AND ("Line Status" <> 'RI')  AND ("Line Status" <> 'RD')
            AND ("Line Status" <> 'VB') THEN
              MaterialDec[3] +=  (((("Material Cost Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant) * Mat1e) * Mat1) * Mat2);
            IF ("Line Status" = 'RI') OR ("Line Status" = 'RD') OR ("Line Status" = 'VB') THEN
              MaterialDec[3] +=  ("Material Cost Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant)
            END;
            '204': BEGIN
            IF ("Line Status" <> 'K') AND ("Line Status" <> 'RI')  AND ("Line Status" <> 'RD')
            AND ("Line Status" <> 'VB') THEN
              MaterialDec[3] +=  (((("Material Cost Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant) * Mat1d) * Mat1) * Mat2);
            IF ("Line Status" = 'RI') OR ("Line Status" = 'RD') OR ("Line Status" = 'VB') THEN
              MaterialDec[3] +=  ("Material Cost Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant)
            END;
            '205': BEGIN
            IF ("Line Status" <> 'K') AND ("Line Status" <> 'RI')  AND ("Line Status" <> 'RD')
            AND ("Line Status" <> 'VB') THEN
              MaterialDec[3] +=  (((("Material Cost Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant) * Mat1f) * Mat1) * Mat2);
            IF ("Line Status" = 'RI') OR ("Line Status" = 'RD') OR ("Line Status" = 'VB') THEN
              MaterialDec[3] +=  ("Material Cost Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant)
            END;
            '206': BEGIN
            IF ("Line Status" <> 'K') AND ("Line Status" <> 'RI')  AND ("Line Status" <> 'RD')
            AND ("Line Status" <> 'VB') THEN
              MaterialDec[3] +=  (((("Material Cost Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant) * Mat1g) * Mat1) * Mat2);
            IF ("Line Status" = 'RI') OR ("Line Status" = 'RD') OR ("Line Status" = 'VB') THEN
              MaterialDec[3] +=  ("Material Cost Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant)
            END;

          END;
        END;
        {IF PrintSubcontract THEN BEGIN
          CASE "Cost Object Subcontracting" OF
            '300': BEGIN
              CASE "Line Status" OF
                'K': SubcontractDec[3] += (((("Subcontracting Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant) * Sub1a) * Sub2a) * Sub3a);
                'I': SubcontractDec[3] += (((("Subcontracting Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant) * Sub1e) * Sub2c) * Sub3c);
                  ELSE
                    SubcontractDec[3] += (((("Subcontracting Amount" *lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant) * Sub1a) * Sub2a) * Sub3a);
              END;
            END;
            '301': SubcontractDec[3] += (((("Subcontracting Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant) * Sub1b) * Sub2a) * Sub3a);
            '302': SubcontractDec[3] += (((("Subcontracting Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant) * Sub1c) * Sub2a) * Sub3a);
            '303': SubcontractDec[3] += (((("Subcontracting Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant) * Sub1f) * Sub2a) * Sub3a);
            '320': SubcontractDec[3] += (((("Subcontracting Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant) * Sub1d) * Sub2b) * Sub3b);
          END;
        END;}
        {IF PrintPlant THEN BEGIN
          CASE  "Cost Object Plant" OF
            '400': PlantDec[3] += (((("Plant Cost Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant) * Plnt1a) * Plnt2a) * Plnt3a);
            '401': PlantDec[3] += (((("Plant Cost Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant) * Plnt1b) * Plnt2a) * Plnt3a);
            '402': PlantDec[3] += (((("Plant Cost Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant) * Plnt1c) * Plnt2a) * Plnt3a);
          END;
        END;}
        IF PrintTotal THEN
          TotalDec[3] += PlantDec[3] + SubcontractDec[3] + MaterialDec[3] + LaborDec[3];
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE InsertTempEstPartRec@1000000018(pVallueDec@1000000000 : ARRAY [8] OF Decimal;SubEstNo@1000000001 : Code[20];Desc@1000000002 : Text[50]);
    BEGIN
      TempSubEstRec."Estimate No." := "Estimate Line NEW"."Estimate No.";
      TempSubEstRec."Sub-Estimate No." := SubEstNo;
      TempSubEstRec.Description := Desc;
      IF TempSubEstRec.INSERT THEN BEGIN
        SubEstCnt += 1;
        TotValueDec[SubEstCnt][1] := pVallueDec[1]; // := Hours    //10;8
        TotValueDec[SubEstCnt][2] := pVallueDec[2]; // := LaborTotal[2];
        TotValueDec[SubEstCnt][3] := pVallueDec[3]; // := MaterialTotal[2];
        TotValueDec[SubEstCnt][4] := pVallueDec[4]; // := SubContractTotal[2];
        TotValueDec[SubEstCnt][5] := pVallueDec[5]; // := PlantTotal[2];
        TotValueDec[SubEstCnt][6] := pVallueDec[6]; // := AmountTotal[2];
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE InsertTempEstPartPartRec@1000000013(pVallueDec@1000000000 : ARRAY [8] OF Decimal;SubEstNo@1000000001 : Code[20];Part@1000000002 : Code[20];Desc@1000000003 : Text[50]);
    BEGIN
      TempEstPartRec."Estimate No." := "Estimate Line NEW"."Estimate No.";
      TempEstPartRec."Sub-Estimate No." := SubEstNo;
      TempEstPartRec."Part Group" := 'G';
      TempEstPartRec.Part := Part;
      TempEstPartRec.Description := Desc;
      IF TempEstPartRec.INSERT THEN BEGIN
        SubEstPartCnt += 1;
        TotValuepDec[SubEstPartCnt][1] := pVallueDec[1]; // := Hours    //10;8
        TotValuepDec[SubEstPartCnt][2] := pVallueDec[2]; // := LaborTotal[2];
        TotValuepDec[SubEstPartCnt][3] := pVallueDec[3]; // := MaterialTotal[2];
        TotValuepDec[SubEstPartCnt][4] := pVallueDec[4]; // := SubContractTotal[2];
        TotValuepDec[SubEstPartCnt][5] := pVallueDec[5]; // := PlantTotal[2];
        TotValuepDec[SubEstPartCnt][6] := pVallueDec[6]; // := AmountTotal[2];
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE PartExist@1000000030(EstNo@1000000000 : Code[20];SubEstNo@1000000002 : Code[20];VAR Prt@1000000001 : Code[20]) : Boolean;
    VAR
      Parts@1000000003 : Record 11012153;
    BEGIN
      //niveau hoger ophalen
      Parts.RESET;
      Parts.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", EstNo);
      Parts.SETRANGE("Sub-Estimate No.",  SubEstNo);
      Parts.SETRANGE("Part Group", 'G');
      Parts.SETRANGE(Part, Prt);
      IF Parts.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
        IF (Parts.Level = 2) OR (Parts.Level = 3) THEN BEGIN
          TempEstPartRec.RESET;
          TempEstPartRec.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", EstNo);
          TempEstPartRec.SETRANGE("Sub-Estimate No.", SubEstNo);
          TempEstPartRec.SETRANGE("Part Group", 'G');
          TempEstPartRec.SETRANGE(Part, Parts.Chapter);
          IF TempEstPartRec.FINDFIRST THEN
            EXIT(TRUE)
          ELSE BEGIN
            Prt := Parts.Chapter;
            EXIT(FALSE);
          END;
        END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE matrix@1000000004(m_col@1000000000 : Integer;m_row@1000000001 : Integer) m_ret : Code[10];
    VAR
      xx@1000000002 : Integer;
      alf@1000000003 : Code[50];
      m_rest@1000000004 : Decimal;
      m_nu@1000000005 : Decimal;
      m_heel@1000000006 : Decimal;
      m_tus@1000000007 : Code[30];
    BEGIN
      IF m_col > 16384 THEN BEGIN
        m_tus := 'XFD';
        ERROR('Selecteer minder kolommen (max 16384)');
      END ELSE BEGIN
        alf := 'ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ ';
        REPEAT
          IF m_col > 676  THEN
            m_heel := ROUND(m_col/(POWER(26.000000001,2)),1,'<')
          ELSE
            m_heel := ROUND(m_col/26.000000001,1,'<');
          IF m_heel > 0 THEN
            m_nu := m_heel
          ELSE
            m_nu := m_col;
          IF m_nu = 0 THEN
            m_nu := 27;
          m_tus := m_tus + COPYSTR(alf,m_nu,1);
          IF m_col > 676 THEN
            m_col := ROUND(m_col-(m_heel*(POWER(26,2))),1)
          ELSE
            m_col := ROUND(m_col-(m_heel*26),1);
        UNTIL m_heel <= 0;
      END;

      m_ret := DELCHR(STRSUBSTNO('%1 %2',m_tus,m_row));
    END;

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function


Shared Data1 as Object

Public Function GetData(Num as Integer, Group as integer) as Object
if Group = 1 then
   Return Cstr(Choose(Num, Split(Cstr(Data1),Chr(177))))
End If
End Function

Public Function SetData(NewData as Object,Group as integer)
  If Group = 1 and NewData &gt; "" Then
      Data1 = NewData
  End If
  Return True
End Function
